## [Jul 28 - Aug 03, 2025](/content/2025/30/README.md)

### Messaging

*   [backlite (‚≠ê102)](https://github.com/mikestefanello/backlite) - Type-safe, persistent, embedded task queues and background job runner w/ SQLite.

## [Jul 21 - Jul 27, 2025](/content/2025/29/README.md)

### Authentication and OAuth

*   [x509proxy (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/vkuznet/x509proxy) - Library to handle X509 proxy certificates.

### Standard CLI

*   [goopt (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/napalu/goopt) - A declarative, struct-tag based CLI framework for Go, with a broad feature set such as hierarchical commands/flags, i18n, shell completion, and validation.

### Queues

*   [dqueue (‚≠ê0)](https://github.com/vodolaz095/dqueue) - Simple, in memory, zero dependency and battle tested, thread-safe deferred queue.

### Pipes

*   [pipelines (‚≠ê11)](https://github.com/nxdir-s/pipelines) - Generic pipeline functions for concurrent processing.

### Relational Database Drivers

*   [go-rqlite (‚≠ê165)](https://github.com/rqlite/gorqlite) - A Go client for rqlite, providing easy-to-use abstractions for working with the rqlite API.

### Distributed Systems

*   [opentelemetry-go-auto-instrumentation (‚≠ê619)](https://github.com/alibaba/opentelemetry-go-auto-instrumentation) - OpenTelemetry Compile-Time Instrumentation for Golang.
*   [outbox (‚≠ê78)](https://github.com/oagudo/outbox) - Lightweight library for the transactional outbox pattern in Go, not tied to any specific relational database or broker.

### Embeddable Scripting Languages

*   [FrankenPHP (‚≠ê9.7k)](https://github.com/dunglas/frankenphp) - PHP embedded in Go, with a `net/http` handler.

### File Handling

*   [fastwalk (‚≠ê98)](https://github.com/charlievieth/fastwalk) - Fast parallel directory traversal library (used by [fzf (‚≠ê72k)](https://github.com/junegunn/fzf)).

### Job Scheduler

*   [cheek (‚≠ê192)](https://github.com/bart6114/cheek) - A simple crontab like scheduler that aims to offer a KISS approach to job scheduling.

### Messaging

*   [GoEventBus (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/Raezil/GoEventBus) - A blazing‚Äëfast, in‚Äëmemory, lock‚Äëfree event bus library

### Networking

*   [nodepass (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/yosebyte/nodepass) - A secure, efficient TCP/UDP tunneling solution that delivers fast, reliable access across network restrictions using pre-established TLS/TCP connections.

### HTTP Clients

*   [go-ipmux (‚≠ê27)](https://github.com/optimus-hft/go-ipmux) - A library for Multiplexing HTTP requests based on multiple Source IPs.

### Reflection

*   [reflectpro (‚≠ê7)](https://github.com/gontainer/reflectpro) - Callers, copiers, getters and setters for go.

### Stream Processing

*   [nibbler (‚≠ê13)](https://github.com/naughtygopher/nibbler) - A lightweight package for micro batch processing.

### Parsers/Encoders/Decoders

*   [godump (goforj) (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/goforj/godump) - Pretty-print Go structs with Laravel/Symfony-style dumps, full type info, colorized CLI output, cycle detection, and private field access.

### Scrapers

*   [go-sitemap-parser (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/aafeher/go-sitemap-parser) - Go language library for parsing Sitemaps.

### Utilities

*   [debounce (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/floatdrop/debounce) - A zero-allocation debouncer written in Go.
*   [lang (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/maxbolgarin/lang) - Generic one-liners to work with variables, slices and maps without boilerplate code.

### UUID

*   [guid (‚≠ê67)](https://github.com/sdrapkin/guid) - Fast cryptographically safe Guid generator for Go (\~10x faster than `uuid`).

### Go Tools / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [gotutor (‚≠ê52)](https://github.com/ahmedakef/gotutor) - Online Go Debugger & Visualizer.

### DevOps Tools / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [dish (‚≠ê244)](https://github.com/thevxn/dish) - A lightweight, remotely configurable monitoring service.

### Guided Learning / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [The Go Interview Practice (‚≠ê482)](https://github.com/RezaSi/go-interview-practice) - A GitHub repository offering coding challenges for Go technical interview preparation.

### Configuration

*   [zerocfg (‚≠ê192)](https://github.com/chaindead/zerocfg) - Zero-effort, concise configuration management that avoids boilerplate and repetitive code, supports multiple sources with priority overrides.

### Databases Implemented in Go

*   [DiceDB (‚≠ê11k)](https://github.com/DiceDB/dice) - An open-source, fast, reactive, in-memory database optimized for modern hardware. Higher throughput and lower median latencies, making it ideal for modern workloads.

### Database Tools

*   [database-gateway (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/kazhuravlev/database-gateway) - Running SQL in production with ACLs, logs, and shared links.

### Error Handling

*   [metaerr (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/quantumcycle/metaerr) - A library to create your custom error builders producing structured errors with metadata from different sources and optional stacktraces.

*   [optional (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/kazhuravlev/optional) - Optional struct fields and vars.

## [Jan 27 - Feb 02, 2025](/content/2025/4/README.md)

### Authentication and OAuth

### Relational Database Drivers

*   [go-sqlite3 (‚≠ê740)](https://github.com/ncruces/go-sqlite3) - This Go module is compatible with the database/sql driver. It allows embedding SQLite into your application, provides direct access to its C API, supports SQLite VFS, and also includes a GORM driver.
*   [sqlite](https://pkg.go.dev/modernc.org/sqlite) - Package sqlite is a sql/database driver using a CGo-free port of the C SQLite3 library.

*   [archives (‚≠ê266)](https://github.com/mholt/archives) - a cross-platform, multi-format Go library for working with archives and compression formats with a unified API and as virtual file systems compatible with io/fs.

### HTTP Clients

*   [axios4go (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/rezmoss/axios4go) - A Go HTTP client library inspired by Axios, providing a simple and intuitive API for making HTTP requests.

### Server Applications

*   [wd-41 (‚≠ê149)](https://github.com/baalimago/wd-41) - A (w)eb (d)evelopment server with automatic live-reload on file changes.

### Template Engines

*   [extemplate](https://git.sr.ht/~dvko/extemplate) - Tiny wrapper around html/template to allow for easy file-based template inheritance.

### Mock

*   [gomock (‚≠ê2.9k)](https://github.com/uber-go/mock) - Mocking framework for the Go programming language.
*   [pgxmock (‚≠ê498)](https://github.com/pashagolub/pgxmock) - A mock library implementing [pgx - PostgreSQL Driver and Toolkit (‚≠ê12k)](https://github.com/jackc/pgx/).

### Formatters

*   [sq (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/neilotoole/sq) - Convert data from SQL databases or document formats like CSV or Excel into formats such as JSON, Excel, CSV, HTML, Markdown, XML, and YAML.

### Utilities

*   [xpool (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/peczenyj/xpool) - Yet another golang type safe object pool using generics.

### XML / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

### Caches

*   [fastcache (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/VictoriaMetrics/fastcache) - fast thread-safe inmemory cache for big number of entries. Minimizes GC overhead.
*   [GCache (‚≠ê2.7k)](https://github.com/bluele/gcache) - Cache library with support for expirable Cache, LFU, LRU and ARC.
*   [gdcache (‚≠ê13)](https://github.com/ulovecode/gdcache) - A pure non-intrusive cache library implemented by golang, you can use it to implement your own distributed cache.
*   [go-mcache (‚≠ê98)](https://github.com/OrlovEvgeny/go-mcache) - Fast in-memory key:value store/cache library. Pointer caches.

*   [buntdb (‚≠ê4.7k)](https://github.com/tidwall/buntdb) - Fast, embeddable, in-memory key/value database for Go with custom indexing and spatial support.

*   [snowball (‚≠ê38)](https://github.com/goodsign/snowball) - Snowball stemmer port (cgo wrapper) for Go. Provides word stem extraction functionality [Snowball native](http://snowball.tartarus.org/).
*   [spaGO (‚≠ê1.8k)](https://github.com/nlpodyssey/spago) - Self-contained Machine Learning and Natural Language Processing library in Go.

### Slugifiers

*   [go-slugify (‚≠ê96)](https://github.com/mozillazg/go-slugify) - Make pretty slug with multiple languages support.
*   [slug (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/gosimple/slug) - URL-friendly slugify with multiple languages support.
*   [Slugify (‚≠ê34)](https://github.com/avelino/slugify) - Go slugify application that handles string.

### Tokenizers

*   [gojieba (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/yanyiwu/gojieba) - This is a Go implementation of [jieba (‚≠ê34k)](https://github.com/fxsjy/jieba) which a Chinese word splitting algorithm.
*   [gotokenizer (‚≠ê21)](https://github.com/xujiajun/gotokenizer) - A tokenizer based on the dictionary and Bigram language models for Golang. (Now only support chinese segmentation)
*   [gse (‚≠ê2.7k)](https://github.com/go-ego/gse) - Go efficient text segmentation; support english, chinese, japanese and other.
*   [MMSEGO (‚≠ê62)](https://github.com/awsong/MMSEGO) - This is a GO implementation of [MMSEG](http://technology.chtsai.org/mmseg/) which a Chinese word splitting algorithm.
*   [prose (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/jdkato/prose) - Library for text processing that supports tokenization, part-of-speech tagging, named-entity extraction, and more. English only.

### Translation

*   [go-i18n (‚≠ê3.3k)](https://github.com/nicksnyder/go-i18n/) - Package and an accompanying tool to work with localized text.
*   [go-mystem (‚≠ê34)](https://github.com/dveselov/mystem) - CGo bindings to Yandex.Mystem - russian morphology analyzer.
*   [go-pinyin (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/mozillazg/go-pinyin) - CN Hanzi to Hanyu Pinyin converter.
*   [gotext (‚≠ê473)](https://github.com/leonelquinteros/gotext) - GNU gettext utilities for Go.
*   [iuliia-go (‚≠ê53)](https://github.com/mehanizm/iuliia-go) - Transliterate Cyrillic ‚Üí Latin in every possible way.
*   [t (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/youthlin/t) - Another i18n pkg for golang, which follows GNU gettext style and supports .po/.mo files: `t.T (gettext)`, `t.N (ngettext)`, etc. And it contains a cmd tool [xtemplate (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/youthlin/t/blob/main/cmd/xtemplate), which can extract messages as a pot file from text/html template.

*   [spinner (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/briandowns/spinner) - Go package to easily provide a terminal spinner with options.
*   [tabby (‚≠ê358)](https://github.com/cheynewallace/tabby) - A tiny library for super simple Golang tables.
*   [table (‚≠ê50)](https://github.com/tomlazar/table) - Small library for terminal color based tables.
*   [termbox-go (‚≠ê4.7k)](https://github.com/nsf/termbox-go) - Termbox is a library for creating cross-platform text-based interfaces.
*   [termdash (‚≠ê2.8k)](https://github.com/mum4k/termdash) - Go terminal dashboard based on **termbox-go** and inspired by [termui (‚≠ê13k)](https://github.com/gizak/termui).
*   [termenv (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/muesli/termenv) - Advanced ANSI style & color support for your terminal applications.
*   [termui (‚≠ê13k)](https://github.com/gizak/termui) - Go terminal dashboard based on **termbox-go** and inspired by [blessed-contrib (‚≠ê16k)](https://github.com/yaronn/blessed-contrib).
*   [uiprogress (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/gosuri/uiprogress) - Flexible library to render progress bars in terminal applications.
*   [uitable (‚≠ê741)](https://github.com/gosuri/uitable) - Library to improve readability in terminal apps using tabular data.
*   [yacspin (‚≠ê449)](https://github.com/theckman/yacspin) - Yet Another CLi Spinner package, for working with terminal spinners.

### Standard CLI

*   [argparse (‚≠ê623)](https://github.com/akamensky/argparse) - Command line argument parser inspired by Python's argparse module.

*   [cmd (‚≠ê43)](https://github.com/posener/cmd) - Extends the standard `flag` package to support sub commands and more in idiomatic way.

*   [Dnote (‚≠ê2.9k)](https://github.com/dnote/dnote) - A simple command line notebook with multi-device sync.
*   [elvish (‚≠ê6.1k)](https://github.com/elves/elvish) - An expressive programming language and a versatile interactive shell.
*   [env (‚≠ê121)](https://github.com/codingconcepts/env) - Tag-based environment configuration for structs.
*   [flaggy (‚≠ê862)](https://github.com/integrii/flaggy) - A robust and idiomatic flags package with excellent subcommand support.
*   [flagvar (‚≠ê45)](https://github.com/sgreben/flagvar) - A collection of flag argument types for Go's standard `flag` package.
*   [go-arg (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/alexflint/go-arg) - Struct-based argument parsing in Go.
*   [go-flags (‚≠ê2.7k)](https://github.com/jessevdk/go-flags) - go command line option parser.
*   [gocmd (‚≠ê66)](https://github.com/devfacet/gocmd) - Go library for building command line applications.
*   [hiboot cli (‚≠ê181)](https://github.com/hidevopsio/hiboot/tree/master/pkg/app/cli) - cli application framework with auto configuration and dependency injection.
*   [job (‚≠ê148)](https://github.com/liujianping/job) - JOB, make your short-term command as a long-term job.
*   [kingpin (‚≠ê3.5k)](https://github.com/alecthomas/kingpin) - Command line and flag parser supporting sub commands (superseded by `kong`; see below).
*   [liner (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/peterh/liner) - Go readline-like library for command-line interfaces.
*   [mow.cli (‚≠ê886)](https://github.com/jawher/mow.cli) - Go library for building CLI applications with sophisticated flag and argument parsing and validation.
*   [ops (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/nanovms/ops) - Unikernel Builder/Orchestrator.
*   [pflag (‚≠ê2.6k)](https://github.com/spf13/pflag) - Drop-in replacement for Go's flag package, implementing POSIX/GNU-style --flags.

*   [strumt (‚≠ê62)](https://github.com/antham/strumt) - Library to create prompt chain.
*   [subcmd (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/bobg/subcmd) - Another approach to parsing and running subcommands. Works alongside the standard `flag` package.
*   [ts (‚≠ê21)](https://github.com/liujianping/ts) - Timestamp convert & compare tool.
*   [ukautz/clif (‚≠ê129)](https://github.com/ukautz/clif) - Small command line interface framework.
*   [urfave/cli (‚≠ê23k)](https://github.com/urfave/cli) - Simple, fast, and fun package for building command line apps in Go (formerly codegangsta/cli).
*   [wlog (‚≠ê67)](https://github.com/dixonwille/wlog) - Simple logging interface that supports cross-platform color and concurrency.

### Configuration

*   [aconfig (‚≠ê594)](https://github.com/cristalhq/aconfig) - Simple, useful and opinionated config loader.
*   [cleanenv (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/ilyakaznacheev/cleanenv) - Minimalistic configuration reader (from files, ENV, and wherever you want).
*   [config (‚≠ê338)](https://github.com/JeremyLoy/config) - Cloud native application configuration. Bind ENV to structs in only two lines.
*   [configuration (‚≠ê108)](https://github.com/BoRuDar/configuration) - Library for initializing configuration structs from env variables, files, flags and 'default' tag.
*   [configure (‚≠ê55)](https://github.com/paked/configure) - Provides configuration through multiple sources, including JSON, flags and environment variables.
*   [configuro (‚≠ê94)](https://github.com/sherifabdlnaby/configuro) - opinionated configuration loading & validation framework from ENV and Files focused towards 12-Factor compliant applications.
*   [confita (‚≠ê505)](https://github.com/heetch/confita) - Load configuration in cascade from multiple backends into a struct.
*   [conflate (‚≠ê36)](https://github.com/the4thamigo-uk/conflate) - Library/tool to merge multiple JSON/YAML/TOML files from arbitrary URLs, validation against a JSON schema, and application of default values defined in the schema.
*   [env (‚≠ê5.6k)](https://github.com/caarlos0/env) - Parse environment variables to Go structs (with defaults).
*   [env (‚≠ê70)](https://github.com/junk1tm/env) - A lightweight package for loading environment variables into structs.
*   [envconfig (‚≠ê244)](https://github.com/vrischmann/envconfig) - Read your configuration from environment variables.
*   [envh (‚≠ê100)](https://github.com/antham/envh) - Helpers to manage environment variables.
*   [fig (‚≠ê381)](https://github.com/kkyr/fig) - Tiny library for reading configuration from a file and from environment variables (with validation & defaults).
*   [genv (‚≠ê42)](https://github.com/sakirsensoy/genv) - Read environment variables easily with dotenv support.
*   [go-aws-ssm (‚≠ê62)](https://github.com/PaddleHQ/go-aws-ssm) - Go package that fetches parameters from AWS System Manager - Parameter Store.
*   [go-conf (‚≠ê11)](https://github.com/ThomasObenaus/go-conf) - Simple library for application configuration based on annotated structs. It supports reading the configuration from environment variables, config files and command line parameters.
*   [go-ini (‚≠ê15)](https://github.com/subpop/go-ini) - A Go package that marshals and unmarshals INI-files.
*   [go-ssm-config (‚≠ê22)](https://github.com/ianlopshire/go-ssm-config) - Go utility for loading configuration parameters from AWS SSM (Parameter Store).
*   [go-up (‚≠ê43)](https://github.com/ufoscout/go-up) - A simple configuration library with recursive placeholders resolution and no magic.
*   [godotenv (‚≠ê9.5k)](https://github.com/joho/godotenv) - Go port of Ruby's dotenv library (Loads environment variables from `.env`).
*   [gofigure (‚≠ê68)](https://github.com/ian-kent/gofigure) - Go application configuration made easy.
*   [gone/jconf (‚≠ê50)](https://github.com/One-com/gone/tree/master/jconf) - Modular JSON configuration. Keep your config structs along with the code they configure and delegate parsing to submodules without sacrificing full config serialization.
*   [gonfig (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/milad-abbasi/gonfig) - Tag-based configuration parser which loads values from different providers into typesafe struct.
*   [gookit/config (‚≠ê558)](https://github.com/gookit/config) - application config manage(load,get,set). support JSON, YAML, TOML, INI, HCL. multi file load, data override merge.
*   [hjson (‚≠ê336)](https://github.com/hjson/hjson-go) - Human JSON, a configuration file format for humans. Relaxed syntax, fewer mistakes, more comments.
*   [hocon (‚≠ê85)](https://github.com/gurkankaymak/hocon) - Configuration library for working with the HOCON(a human-friendly JSON superset) format, supports features like environment variables, referencing other values, comments and multiple files.
*   [ingo (‚≠ê40)](https://github.com/schachmat/ingo) - Flags persisted in an ini-like config file.
*   [ini (‚≠ê3.5k)](https://github.com/go-ini/ini) - Go package to read and write INI files.
*   [ini (‚≠ê17)](https://github.com/wlevene/ini) - INI Parser & Write Library, Unmarshal to Struct, Marshal to Json, Write File, watch file.
*   [joshbetz/config (‚≠ê215)](https://github.com/joshbetz/config) - Small configuration library for Go that parses environment variables, JSON files, and reloads automatically on SIGHUP.
*   [kelseyhightower/envconfig (‚≠ê5.3k)](https://github.com/kelseyhightower/envconfig) - Go library for managing configuration data from environment variables.
*   [koanf (‚≠ê3.3k)](https://github.com/knadh/koanf) - Light weight, extensible library for reading config in Go applications. Built in support for JSON, TOML, YAML, env, command line.
*   [konfig (‚≠ê645)](https://github.com/lalamove/konfig) - Composable, observable and performant config handling for Go for the distributed processing era.
*   [mini (‚≠ê37)](https://github.com/sasbury/mini) - Golang package for parsing ini-style configuration files.
*   [nasermirzaei89/env (‚≠ê18)](https://github.com/nasermirzaei89/env) - Simple useful package for read environment variables.
*   [onion (‚≠ê118)](https://github.com/goraz/onion) - Layer based configuration for Go, Supports JSON, TOML, YAML, properties, etcd, env, and encryption using PGP.
*   [piper (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/Yiling-J/piper) - Viper wrapper with config inheritance and key generation.
*   [store (‚≠ê275)](https://github.com/tucnak/store) - Lightweight configuration manager for Go.
*   [swap (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/oblq/swap) - Instantiate/configure structs recursively, based on build environment. (YAML, TOML, JSON and env).
*   [typenv (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/diegomarangoni/typenv) - Minimalistic, zero dependency, typed environment variables library.
*   [uConfig (‚≠ê72)](https://github.com/omeid/uconfig) - Lightweight, zero-dependency, and extendable configuration management.
*   [viper (‚≠ê29k)](https://github.com/spf13/viper) - Go configuration with fangs.
*   [xdg (‚≠ê843)](https://github.com/adrg/xdg) - Go implementation of the [XDG Base Directory Specification](https://specifications.freedesktop.org/basedir-spec/latest/) and [XDG user directories](https://wiki.archlinux.org/index.php/XDG_user_directories).

### Miscellaneous Data Structures and Algorithms

*   [concurrent-writer (‚≠ê57)](https://github.com/free/concurrent-writer) - Highly concurrent drop-in replacement for `bufio.Writer`.
*   [count-min-log (‚≠ê67)](https://github.com/seiflotfy/count-min-log) - Go implementation Count-Min-Log sketch: Approximately counting with approximate counters (Like Count-Min sketch but using less memory).
*   [fsm (‚≠ê80)](https://github.com/cocoonspace/fsm) - Finite-State Machine package.
*   [go-geoindex (‚≠ê358)](https://github.com/hailocab/go-geoindex) - In-memory geo index.
*   [go-rquad (‚≠ê137)](https://github.com/aurelien-rainone/go-rquad) - Region quadtrees with efficient point location and neighbour finding.
*   [gofal (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/xxjwxc/gofal) - fractional api for Go.
*   [gota (‚≠ê3.2k)](https://github.com/kniren/gota) - Implementation of dataframes, series, and data wrangling methods for Go.
*   [hide (‚≠ê70)](https://github.com/emvi/hide) - ID type with marshalling to/from hash to prevent sending IDs to clients.
*   [hyperloglog (‚≠ê985)](https://github.com/axiomhq/hyperloglog) - HyperLogLog implementation with Sparse, LogLog-Beta bias correction and TailCut space reduction.

### Text Analysis

### Databases Implemented in Go

*   [cockroach (‚≠ê31k)](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach) - Scalable, Geo-Replicated, Transactional Datastore.

*   [Databunker (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/paranoidguy/databunker) - Personally identifiable information (PII) storage service built to comply with GDPR and CCPA.

*   [eliasdb (‚≠ê1k)](https://github.com/krotik/eliasdb) - Dependency-free, transactional graph database with REST API, phrase search and SQL-like query language.
*   [godis (‚≠ê3.7k)](https://github.com/hdt3213/godis) - A Golang implemented high-performance Redis server and cluster.
*   [goleveldb (‚≠ê6.3k)](https://github.com/syndtr/goleveldb) - Implementation of the [LevelDB (‚≠ê38k)](https://github.com/google/leveldb) key/value database in Go.
*   [hare (‚≠ê97)](https://github.com/jameycribbs/hare) - A simple database management system that stores each table as a text file of line-delimited JSON.
*   [immudb (‚≠ê8.8k)](https://github.com/codenotary/immudb) - immudb is a lightweight, high-speed immutable database for systems and applications written in Go.
*   [influxdb (‚≠ê30k)](https://github.com/influxdb/influxdb) - Scalable datastore for metrics, events, and real-time analytics.
*   [ledisdb (‚≠ê4.1k)](https://github.com/siddontang/ledisdb) - Ledisdb is a high performance NoSQL like Redis based on LevelDB.
*   [levigo (‚≠ê419)](https://github.com/jmhodges/levigo) - Levigo is a Go wrapper for LevelDB.
*   [lotusdb (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/flower-corp/lotusdb) - Fast k/v database compatible with lsm and b+tree.
*   [Milvus (‚≠ê36k)](https://github.com/milvus-io/milvus) - Milvus is a vector database for embedding management, analytics and search.
*   [moss (‚≠ê1k)](https://github.com/couchbase/moss) - Moss is a simple LSM key-value storage engine written in 100% Go.
*   [piladb (‚≠ê207)](https://github.com/fern4lvarez/piladb) - Lightweight RESTful database engine based on stack data structures.
*   [pogreb (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/akrylysov/pogreb) - Embedded key-value store for read-heavy workloads.
*   [prometheus (‚≠ê60k)](https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus) - Monitoring system and time series database.
*   [rosedb (‚≠ê4.8k)](https://github.com/roseduan/rosedb) - An embedded k-v database based on LSM+WAL, supports string, list, hash, set, zset.
*   [rqlite (‚≠ê17k)](https://github.com/rqlite/rqlite) - The lightweight, distributed, relational database built on SQLite.
*   [tempdb (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/rafaeljesus/tempdb) - Key-value store for temporary items.
*   [tidb (‚≠ê39k)](https://github.com/pingcap/tidb) - TiDB is a distributed SQL database. Inspired by the design of Google F1.
*   [tiedot (‚≠ê2.7k)](https://github.com/HouzuoGuo/tiedot) - Your NoSQL database powered by Golang.
*   [Vasto (‚≠ê263)](https://github.com/chrislusf/vasto) - A distributed high-performance key-value store. On Disk. Eventual consistent. HA. Able to grow or shrink without service interruption.
*   [VictoriaMetrics (‚≠ê15k)](https://github.com/VictoriaMetrics/VictoriaMetrics) - fast, resource-effective and scalable open source time series database. May be used as long-term remote storage for Prometheus. Supports PromQL.

### Database Schema Migration

*   [atlas (‚≠ê7k)](https://github.com/ariga/atlas) - A Database Toolkit. A CLI designed to help companies better work with their data.
*   [avro (‚≠ê47)](https://github.com/khezen/avro) - Discover SQL schemas and convert them to AVRO schemas. Query SQL records into AVRO bytes.
*   [darwin (‚≠ê149)](https://github.com/GuiaBolso/darwin) - Database schema evolution library for Go.
*   [go-fixtures (‚≠ê30)](https://github.com/RichardKnop/go-fixtures) - Django style fixtures for Golang's excellent built-in database/sql library.
*   [go-pg-migrate (‚≠ê11)](https://github.com/lawzava/go-pg-migrate) - CLI-friendly package for go-pg migrations management.
*   [go-pg-migrations (‚≠ê86)](https://github.com/robinjoseph08/go-pg-migrations) - A Go package to help write migrations with go-pg/pg.
*   [goavro (‚≠ê1k)](https://github.com/linkedin/goavro) - A Go package that encodes and decodes Avro data.
*   [goose (‚≠ê8.7k)](https://github.com/pressly/goose) - Database migration tool. You can manage your database's evolution by creating incremental SQL or Go scripts.
*   [gormigrate (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/go-gormigrate/gormigrate) - Database schema migration helper for Gorm ORM.
*   [migrate (‚≠ê17k)](https://github.com/golang-migrate/migrate) - Database migrations. CLI and Golang library.
*   [migrator (‚≠ê178)](https://github.com/lopezator/migrator) - Dead simple Go database migration library.
*   [migrator (‚≠ê25)](https://github.com/larapulse/migrator) - MySQL database migrator designed to run migrations to your features and manage database schema update with intuitive go code.
*   [schema (‚≠ê42)](https://github.com/adlio/schema) - Library to embed schema migrations for database/sql-compatible databases inside your Go binaries.
*   [skeema (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/skeema/skeema) - Pure-SQL schema management system for MySQL, with support for sharding and external online schema change tools.
*   [soda (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/gobuffalo/pop/tree/master/soda) - Database migration, creation, ORM, etc... for MySQL, PostgreSQL, and SQLite.
*   [sql-migrate (‚≠ê3.4k)](https://github.com/rubenv/sql-migrate) - Database migration tool. Allows embedding migrations into the application using go-bindata.
*   [sqlize (‚≠ê122)](https://github.com/sunary/sqlize) - Database migration generator. Allows generate sql migration from model and existing sql by differ them.

### Database Tools

*   [chproxy (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/Vertamedia/chproxy) - HTTP proxy for ClickHouse database.
*   [dbbench (‚≠ê109)](https://github.com/sj14/dbbench) - Database benchmarking tool with support for several databases and scripts.
*   [go-mysql (‚≠ê4.8k)](https://github.com/siddontang/go-mysql) - Go toolset to handle MySQL protocol and replication.
*   [octillery (‚≠ê199)](https://github.com/knocknote/octillery) - Go package for sharding databases ( Supports every ORM or raw SQL ).
*   [pg\_timetable (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/cybertec-postgresql/pg_timetable) - Advanced scheduling for PostgreSQL.
*   [pgweb (‚≠ê8.9k)](https://github.com/sosedoff/pgweb) - Web-based PostgreSQL database browser.
*   [prep (‚≠ê35)](https://github.com/hexdigest/prep) - Use prepared SQL statements without changing your code.
*   [pREST (‚≠ê4.4k)](https://github.com/prest/prest) - Simplify and accelerate development, ‚ö° instant, realtime, high-performance on any Postgres application, existing or new.
*   [rwdb (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/andizzle/rwdb) - rwdb provides read replica capability for multiple database servers setup.
*   [vitess (‚≠ê20k)](https://github.com/youtube/vitess) - vitess provides servers and tools which facilitate scaling of MySQL databases for large scale web services.

### SQL Query Builders

*   [bqb (‚≠ê172)](https://github.com/nullism/bqb) - Lightweight and easy to learn query builder.

*   [gendry (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/didi/gendry) - Non-invasive SQL builder and powerful data binder.
*   [godbal (‚≠ê59)](https://github.com/xujiajun/godbal) - Database Abstraction Layer (dbal) for go. Support SQL builder and get result easily.

*   [igor (‚≠ê126)](https://github.com/galeone/igor) - Abstraction layer for PostgreSQL that supports advanced functionality and uses gorm-like syntax.
*   [jet (‚≠ê3.3k)](https://github.com/go-jet/jet) - Framework for writing type-safe SQL queries in Go, with ability to easily convert database query result into desired arbitrary object structure.
*   [ormlite (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/pupizoid/ormlite) - Lightweight package containing some ORM-like features and helpers for sqlite databases.
*   [ozzo-dbx (‚≠ê651)](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-dbx) - Powerful data retrieval methods as well as DB-agnostic query building capabilities.
*   [qry (‚≠ê35)](https://github.com/HnH/qry) - Tool that generates constants from files with raw SQL queries.
*   [sq (‚≠ê201)](https://github.com/bokwoon95/go-structured-query) - Type-safe SQL builder and struct mapper for Go.
*   [sqlf (‚≠ê180)](https://github.com/leporo/sqlf) - Fast SQL query builder.
*   [sqlingo (‚≠ê429)](https://github.com/lqs/sqlingo) - A lightweight DSL to build SQL in Go.
*   [sqrl (‚≠ê281)](https://github.com/elgris/sqrl) - SQL query builder, fork of Squirrel with improved performance.
*   [Squalus](https://gitlab.com/qosenergy/squalus) - Thin layer over the Go SQL package that makes it easier to perform queries.
*   [Squirrel (‚≠ê7.5k)](https://github.com/Masterminds/squirrel) - Go library that helps you build SQL queries.
*   [xo (‚≠ê3.8k)](https://github.com/knq/xo) - Generate idiomatic Go code for databases based on existing schema definitions or custom queries supporting PostgreSQL, MySQL, SQLite, Oracle, and Microsoft SQL Server.

### Error Handling

*   [errors (‚≠ê200)](https://github.com/emperror/errors) - Drop-in replacement for the standard library errors package and github.com/pkg/errors. Provides various error handling primitives.

*   [tracerr (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/ztrue/tracerr) - Golang errors with stack trace and source fragments.

*   [higgs (‚≠ê24)](https://github.com/dastoori/higgs) - A tiny cross-platform Go library to hide/unhide files and directories.
*   [notify (‚≠ê917)](https://github.com/rjeczalik/notify) - File system event notification library with simple API, similar to os/signal.
*   [opc (‚≠ê75)](https://github.com/qmuntal/opc) - Load Open Packaging Conventions (OPC) files for Go.
*   [parquet (‚≠ê118)](https://github.com/parsyl/parquet) - Read and write [parquet](https://parquet.apache.org) files.

*   [pdfcpu (‚≠ê7.8k)](https://github.com/pdfcpu/pdfcpu) - PDF processor.
*   [skywalker (‚≠ê103)](https://github.com/dixonwille/skywalker) - Package to allow one to concurrently go through a filesystem with ease.
*   [todotxt (‚≠ê25)](https://github.com/1set/todotxt) - Go library for Gina Trapani's [*todo.txt*](http://todotxt.org/) files, supports parsing and manipulating of task lists in the [*todo.txt* format](https://github.com/todotxt/todo.txt).
*   [vfs (‚≠ê345)](https://github.com/C2FO/vfs) - A pluggable, extensible, and opinionated set of filesystem functionality for Go across a number of filesystem types such as os, S3, and GCS.

*   [orderbook (‚≠ê498)](https://github.com/i25959341/orderbook) - Matching Engine for Limit Order Book in Golang.

*   [sleet (‚≠ê140)](https://github.com/BoltApp/sleet) - One unified interface for multiple Payment Service Providers (PsP) to process online payment.
*   [techan (‚≠ê868)](https://github.com/sdcoffey/techan) - Technical analysis library with advanced market analysis and trading strategies.
*   [ticker (‚≠ê5.3k)](https://github.com/achannarasappa/ticker) - Terminal stock watcher and stock position tracker.
*   [transaction (‚≠ê136)](https://github.com/claygod/transaction) - Embedded transactional database of accounts, running in multithreaded mode.
*   [vat (‚≠ê115)](https://github.com/dannyvankooten/vat) - VAT number validation & EU VAT rates.

### Forms

*   [bind (‚≠ê32)](https://github.com/robfig/bind) - Bind form data to any Go values.
*   [conform (‚≠ê325)](https://github.com/leebenson/conform) - Keeps user input in check. Trims, sanitizes & scrubs data based on struct tags.
*   [form (‚≠ê848)](https://github.com/go-playground/form) - Decodes url.Values into Go value(s) and Encodes Go value(s) into url.Values. Dual Array and Full map support.
*   [formam (‚≠ê192)](https://github.com/monoculum/formam) - decode form's values into a struct.
*   [forms (‚≠ê142)](https://github.com/albrow/forms) - Framework-agnostic library for parsing and validating form/JSON data which supports multipart forms and files.
*   [gorilla/csrf (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/gorilla/csrf) - CSRF protection for Go web applications & services.
*   [nosurf (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/justinas/nosurf) - CSRF protection middleware for Go.
*   [qs (‚≠ê78)](https://github.com/sonh/qs) - Go module for encoding structs into URL query parameters.
*   [queryparam (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/tomwright/queryparam) - Decode `url.Values` into usable struct values of standard or custom types.

### Goroutines

*   [ants (‚≠ê14k)](https://github.com/panjf2000/ants) - A high-performance and low-cost goroutine pool in Go.
*   [artifex (‚≠ê212)](https://github.com/borderstech/artifex) - Simple in-memory job queue for Golang using worker-based dispatching.
*   [async (‚≠ê249)](https://github.com/reugn/async) - An alternative sync library for Go (Future, Promise, Locks).
*   [async (‚≠ê139)](https://github.com/studiosol/async) - A safe way to execute functions asynchronously, recovering them in case of panic.
*   [breaker (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/kamilsk/breaker) - Flexible mechanism to make execution flow interruptible.
*   [channelify (‚≠ê33)](https://github.com/ddelizia/channelify) - Transform your function to return channels for easy and powerful parallel processing.
*   [concurrency-limiter (‚≠ê18)](https://github.com/vivek-ng/concurrency-limiter) - Concurrency limiter with support for timeouts, dynamic priority and context cancellation of goroutines.
*   [conexec (‚≠ê18)](https://github.com/ITcathyh/conexec) - A concurrent toolkit to help execute funcs concurrently in an efficient and safe way. It supports specifying the overall timeout to avoid blocking and uses goroutine pool to improve efficiency.
*   [cyclicbarrier (‚≠ê153)](https://github.com/marusama/cyclicbarrier) - CyclicBarrier for golang.
*   [execpool (‚≠ê29)](https://github.com/hexdigest/execpool) - A pool built around exec.Cmd that spins up a given number of processes in advance and attaches stdin and stdout to them when needed. Very similar to FastCGI or Apache Prefork MPM but works for any command.
*   [go-floc (‚≠ê268)](https://github.com/workanator/go-floc) - Orchestrate goroutines with ease.
*   [go-flow (‚≠ê222)](https://github.com/kamildrazkiewicz/go-flow) - Control goroutines execution order.
*   [go-tools/multithreading (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/nikhilsaraf/go-tools) - Manage a pool of goroutines using this lightweight library with a simple API.
*   [go-trylock (‚≠ê37)](https://github.com/subchen/go-trylock) - TryLock support on read-write lock for Golang.
*   [go-waitgroup (‚≠ê49)](https://github.com/pieterclaerhout/go-waitgroup) - Like `sync.WaitGroup` with error handling and concurrency control.
*   [go-workers (‚≠ê166)](https://github.com/catmullet/go-workers) - Easily and safely run workers for large data processing pipelines.
*   [goccm (‚≠ê73)](https://github.com/zenthangplus/goccm) - Go Concurrency Manager package limits the number of goroutines that allowed to run concurrently.
*   [gohive (‚≠ê53)](https://github.com/loveleshsharma/gohive) - A highly performant and easy to use Goroutine pool for Go.
*   [gollback (‚≠ê124)](https://github.com/vardius/gollback) - asynchronous simple function utilities, for managing execution of closures and callbacks.
*   [gowl (‚≠ê70)](https://github.com/hamed-yousefi/gowl) - Gowl is a process management and process monitoring tool at once. An infinite worker pool gives you the ability to control the pool and processes and monitor their status.
*   [goworker (‚≠ê2.8k)](https://github.com/benmanns/goworker) - goworker is a Go-based background worker.
*   [gowp (‚≠ê526)](https://github.com/xxjwxc/gowp) - gowp is concurrency limiting goroutine pool.
*   [gpool (‚≠ê90)](https://github.com/Sherifabdlnaby/gpool) - manages a resizeable pool of context-aware goroutines to bound concurrency.
*   [grpool (‚≠ê744)](https://github.com/ivpusic/grpool) - Lightweight Goroutine pool.
*   [hands (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/duanckham/hands) - A process controller used to control the execution and return strategies of multiple goroutines.
*   [Hunch (‚≠ê105)](https://github.com/AaronJan/Hunch) - Hunch provides functions like: `All`, `First`, `Retry`, `Waterfall` etc., that makes asynchronous flow control more intuitive.
*   [kyoo (‚≠ê50)](https://github.com/dirkaholic/kyoo) - Provides an unlimited job queue and concurrent worker pools.
*   [neilotoole/errgroup (‚≠ê165)](https://github.com/neilotoole/errgroup) - Drop-in alternative to `sync/errgroup`, limited to a pool of N worker goroutines.
*   [nursery (‚≠ê69)](https://github.com/arunsworld/nursery) - Structured concurrency in Go.
*   [parallel-fn (‚≠ê37)](https://github.com/rafaeljesus/parallel-fn) - Run functions in parallel.
*   [pond (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/alitto/pond) - Minimalistic and High-performance goroutine worker pool written in Go.
*   [pool (‚≠ê729)](https://github.com/go-playground/pool) - Limited consumer goroutine or unlimited goroutine pool for easier goroutine handling and cancellation.
*   [routine (‚≠ê62)](https://github.com/x-mod/routine) - go routine control with context, support: Main, Go, Pool and some useful Executors.
*   [semaphore (‚≠ê103)](https://github.com/kamilsk/semaphore) - Semaphore pattern implementation with timeout of lock/unlock operations based on channel and context.
*   [semaphore (‚≠ê178)](https://github.com/marusama/semaphore) - Fast resizable semaphore implementation based on CAS (faster than channel-based semaphore implementations).
*   [stl (‚≠ê30)](https://github.com/ssgreg/stl) - Software transactional locks based on Software Transactional Memory (STM) concurrency control mechanism.
*   [threadpool (‚≠ê104)](https://github.com/shettyh/threadpool) - Golang threadpool implementation.
*   [tunny (‚≠ê4k)](https://github.com/Jeffail/tunny) - Goroutine pool for golang.
*   [worker-pool (‚≠ê92)](https://github.com/vardius/worker-pool) - goworker is a Go simple async worker pool.
*   [workerpool (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/gammazero/workerpool) - Goroutine pool that limits the concurrency of task execution, not the number of tasks queued.

### Job Scheduler

*   [clockwerk (‚≠ê181)](https://github.com/onatm/clockwerk) - Go package to schedule periodic jobs using a simple, fluent syntax.
*   [cronticker (‚≠ê18)](https://github.com/krayzpipes/cronticker) - A ticker implementation to support cron schedules.
*   [go-cron (‚≠ê238)](https://github.com/rk/go-cron) - Simple Cron library for go that can execute closures or functions at varying intervals, from once a second to once a year on a specific date and time. Primarily for web applications and long running daemons.
*   [go-quartz (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/reugn/go-quartz) - Simple, zero-dependency scheduling library for Go.
*   [gocron (‚≠ê6.4k)](https://github.com/go-co-op/gocron) - Easy and fluent Go job scheduling. This is an actively maintained fork of [jasonlvhit/gocron (‚≠ê3.5k)](https://github.com/jasonlvhit/gocron).
*   [gron (‚≠ê1k)](https://github.com/roylee0704/gron) - Define time-based tasks using a simple Go API and Gron‚Äôs scheduler will run them accordingly.
*   [gronx (‚≠ê456)](https://github.com/adhocore/gronx) - Cron expression parser, task runner and daemon consuming crontab like task list.
*   [JobRunner (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/bamzi/jobrunner) - Smart and featureful cron job scheduler with job queuing and live monitoring built in.
*   [leprechaun (‚≠ê105)](https://github.com/kilgaloon/leprechaun) - Job scheduler that supports webhooks, crons and classic scheduling.
*   [sched (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/romshark/sched) - A job scheduler with the ability to fast-forward time.
*   [scheduler (‚≠ê470)](https://github.com/carlescere/scheduler) - Cronjobs scheduling made easy.
*   [tasks (‚≠ê313)](https://github.com/madflojo/tasks) - An easy to use in-process scheduler for recurring tasks in Go.

### JSON

*   [ajson (‚≠ê276)](https://github.com/spyzhov/ajson) - Abstract JSON for golang with JSONPath support.
*   [ask (‚≠ê53)](https://github.com/simonnilsson/ask) - Easy access to nested values in maps and slices. Works in combination with encoding/json and other packages that "Unmarshal" arbitrary data into Go data-types.
*   [dynjson (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/cocoonspace/dynjson) - Client-customizable JSON formats for dynamic APIs.
*   [ej (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/lucassscaravelli/ej) - Write and read JSON from different sources succinctly.
*   [epoch (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/vtopc/epoch) - Contains primitives for marshaling/unmarshalling Unix timestamp/epoch to/from build-in time.Time type in JSON.
*   [fastjson (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/valyala/fastjson) - Fast JSON parser and validator for Go. No custom structs, no code generation, no reflection.
*   [gjo (‚≠ê130)](https://github.com/skanehira/gjo) - Small utility to create JSON objects.
*   [GJSON (‚≠ê15k)](https://github.com/tidwall/gjson) - Get a JSON value with one line of code.
*   [go-jsonerror (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/ddymko/go-jsonerror) - Go-JsonError is meant to allow us to easily create json response errors that follow the JsonApi spec.
*   [go-respond (‚≠ê54)](https://github.com/nicklaw5/go-respond) - Go package for handling common HTTP JSON responses.
*   [gojq (‚≠ê189)](https://github.com/elgs/gojq) - JSON query in Golang.
*   [gojson (‚≠ê2.7k)](https://github.com/ChimeraCoder/gojson) - Automatically generate Go (golang) struct definitions from example JSON.
*   [JayDiff (‚≠ê109)](https://github.com/yazgazan/jaydiff) - JSON diff utility written in Go.
*   [jettison (‚≠ê178)](https://github.com/wI2L/jettison) - Fast and flexible JSON encoder for Go.
*   [jscan (‚≠ê95)](https://github.com/romshark/jscan) - High performance zero-allocation JSON iterator.
*   [JSON-to-Go](https://mholt.github.io/json-to-go/) - Convert JSON to Go struct.
*   [JSON-to-Proto](https://json-to-proto.github.io/) - Convert JSON to Protobuf online.
*   [json2go (‚≠ê136)](https://github.com/m-zajac/json2go) - Advanced JSON to Go struct conversion. Provides package that can parse multiple JSON documents and create struct to fit them all.
*   [jsonapi-errors (‚≠ê13)](https://github.com/AmuzaTkts/jsonapi-errors) - Go bindings based on the JSON API errors reference.
*   [jsoncolor (‚≠ê47)](https://github.com/neilotoole/jsoncolor) - Drop-in replacement for `encoding/json` that outputs colorized JSON.
*   [jsondiff (‚≠ê590)](https://github.com/wI2L/jsondiff) - JSON diff library for Go based on RFC6902 (JSON Patch).
*   [jsonf (‚≠ê65)](https://github.com/miolini/jsonf) - Console tool for highlighted formatting and struct query fetching JSON.
*   [jsongo (‚≠ê108)](https://github.com/ricardolonga/jsongo) - Fluent API to make it easier to create Json objects.
*   [jsonhal (‚≠ê14)](https://github.com/RichardKnop/jsonhal) - Simple Go package to make custom structs marshal into HAL compatible JSON responses.
*   [jsonic (‚≠ê11)](https://github.com/sinhashubham95/jsonic) - Utilities to handle and query JSON without defining structs in a type safe manner.
*   [jzon (‚≠ê11)](https://github.com/zerosnake0/jzon) - JSON library with standard compatible API/behavior.
*   [kazaam (‚≠ê286)](https://github.com/Qntfy/kazaam) - API for arbitrary transformation of JSON documents.
*   [mapslice-json (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/mickep76/mapslice-json) - Go MapSlice for ordered marshal/ unmarshal of maps in JSON.
*   [mp (‚≠ê47)](https://github.com/sanbornm/mp) - Simple cli email parser. It currently takes stdin and outputs JSON.
*   [OjG (‚≠ê904)](https://github.com/ohler55/ojg) - Optimized JSON for Go is a high performance parser with a variety of additional JSON tools including JSONPath.
*   [omg.jsonparser (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/dedalqq/omg.jsonparser) - Simple JSON parser with validation by condition via golang struct fields tags.
*   [ujson (‚≠ê82)](https://github.com/olvrng/ujson) - Fast and minimal JSON parser and transformer that works on unstructured JSON.
*   [vjson (‚≠ê40)](https://github.com/miladibra10/vjson) - Go package for validating JSON objects with declaring a JSON schema with fluent API.

### Logging

*   [distillog (‚≠ê31)](https://github.com/amoghe/distillog) - distilled levelled logging (think of it as stdlib + log levels).
*   [glg (‚≠ê190)](https://github.com/kpango/glg) - glg is simple and fast leveled logging library for Go.
*   [glo (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/lajosbencz/glo) - PHP Monolog inspired logging facility with identical severity levels.
*   [glog (‚≠ê3.6k)](https://github.com/golang/glog) - Leveled execution logs for Go.
*   [go-cronowriter (‚≠ê57)](https://github.com/utahta/go-cronowriter) - Simple writer that rotate log files automatically based on current date and time, like cronolog.
*   [go-log (‚≠ê14)](https://github.com/subchen/go-log) - Simple and configurable Logging in Go, with level, formatters and writers.
*   [go-log (‚≠ê35)](https://github.com/siddontang/go-log) - Log lib supports level and multi handlers.
*   [go-log (‚≠ê42)](https://github.com/ian-kent/go-log) - Log4j implementation in Go.
*   [go-logger (‚≠ê289)](https://github.com/apsdehal/go-logger) - Simple logger of Go Programs, with level handlers.
*   [gone/log (‚≠ê50)](https://github.com/One-com/gone/tree/master/log) - Fast, extendable, full-featured, std-lib source compatible log library.
*   [httpretty (‚≠ê408)](https://github.com/henvic/httpretty) - Pretty-prints your regular HTTP requests on your terminal for debugging (similar to http.DumpRequest).
*   [journald (‚≠ê43)](https://github.com/ssgreg/journald) - Go implementation of systemd Journal's native API for logging.
*   [kemba (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/clok/kemba) - A tiny debug logging tool inspired by [debug (‚≠ê11k)](https://github.com/visionmedia/debug), great for CLI tools and applications.
*   [log (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/aerogo/log) - An O(1) logging system that allows you to connect one log to multiple writers (e.g. stdout, a file and a TCP connection).
*   [log (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/apex/log) - Structured logging package for Go.
*   [log (‚≠ê295)](https://github.com/go-playground/log) - Simple, configurable and scalable Structured Logging for Go.
*   [log (‚≠ê26)](https://github.com/teris-io/log) - Structured log interface for Go cleanly separates logging facade from its implementation.
*   [log15 (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/inconshreveable/log15) - Simple, powerful logging for Go.
*   [logdump (‚≠ê11)](https://github.com/ewwwwwqm/logdump) - Package for multi-level logging.
*   [logex (‚≠ê42)](https://github.com/chzyer/logex) - Golang log lib, supports tracking and level, wrap by standard log lib.
*   [logger (‚≠ê156)](https://github.com/azer/logger) - Minimalistic logging library for Go.
*   [logo (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/mbndr/logo) - Golang logger to different configurable writers.
*   [logrus (‚≠ê25k)](https://github.com/Sirupsen/logrus) - Structured logger for Go.
*   [logrusiowriter (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/cabify/logrusiowriter) - `io.Writer` implementation using [logrus (‚≠ê25k)](https://github.com/sirupsen/logrus) logger.
*   [logrusly (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/sebest/logrusly) - [logrus (‚≠ê25k)](https://github.com/sirupsen/logrus) plug-in to send errors to a [Loggly](https://www.loggly.com/).
*   [logur (‚≠ê205)](https://github.com/logur/logur) - An opinionated logger interface and collection of logging best practices with adapters and integrations for well-known libraries ([logrus (‚≠ê25k)](https://github.com/sirupsen/logrus), [go-kit log (‚≠ê27k)](https://github.com/go-kit/kit/tree/master/log), [zap (‚≠ê23k)](https://github.com/uber-go/zap), [zerolog (‚≠ê12k)](https://github.com/rs/zerolog), etc).
*   [logutils (‚≠ê367)](https://github.com/hashicorp/logutils) - Utilities for slightly better logging in Go (Golang) extending the standard logger.
*   [logxi (‚≠ê358)](https://github.com/mgutz/logxi) - 12-factor app logger that is fast and makes you happy.
*   [lumberjack (‚≠ê5.2k)](https://github.com/natefinch/lumberjack) - Simple rolling logger, implements io.WriteCloser.
*   [mlog (‚≠ê33)](https://github.com/jbrodriguez/mlog) - Simple logging module for go, with 5 levels, an optional rotating logfile feature and stdout/stderr output.
*   [noodlog (‚≠ê44)](https://github.com/gyozatech/noodlog) - Parametrized JSON logging library which lets you obfuscate sensitive data and marshal any kind of content. No more printed pointers instead of values, nor escape chars for the JSON strings.
*   [onelog (‚≠ê412)](https://github.com/francoispqt/onelog) - Onelog is a dead simple but very efficient JSON logger. It is the fastest JSON logger out there in all scenarios. Also, it is one of the logger with the lowest allocation.
*   [ozzo-log (‚≠ê123)](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-log) - High performance logging supporting log severity, categorization, and filtering. Can send filtered log messages to various targets (e.g. console, network, mail).
*   [rollingwriter (‚≠ê298)](https://github.com/arthurkiller/rollingWriter) - RollingWriter is an auto-rotate `io.Writer` implementation with multi policies to provide log file rotation.
*   [seelog (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/cihub/seelog) - Logging functionality with flexible dispatching, filtering, and formatting.
*   [spew (‚≠ê6.3k)](https://github.com/davecgh/go-spew) - Implements a deep pretty printer for Go data structures to aid in debugging.
*   [stdlog (‚≠ê48)](https://github.com/alexcesaro/log) - Stdlog is an object-oriented library providing leveled logging. It is very useful for cron jobs.
*   [structy/log (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/structy/log) - A simple to use log system, minimalist but with features for debugging and differentiation of messages.
*   [tail (‚≠ê2.8k)](https://github.com/hpcloud/tail) - Go package striving to emulate the features of the BSD tail program.
*   [xlog (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/xfxdev/xlog) - Plugin architecture and flexible log system for Go, with level ctrl, multiple log target and custom log format.
*   [xlog (‚≠ê139)](https://github.com/rs/xlog) - Structured logger for `net/context` aware HTTP handlers with flexible dispatching.
*   [yell (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/jfcg/yell) - Yet another minimalistic logging library.
*   [zap (‚≠ê23k)](https://github.com/uber-go/zap) - Fast, structured, leveled logging in Go.
*   [zerolog (‚≠ê12k)](https://github.com/rs/zerolog) - Zero-allocation JSON logger.
*   [zkits-logger (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/edoger/zkits-logger) - A powerful zero-dependency JSON logger.

*   [gorgonia (‚≠ê5.8k)](https://github.com/gorgonia/gorgonia) - graph-based computational library like Theano for Go that provides primitives for building various machine learning and neural network algorithms.
*   [gorse (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/zhenghaoz/gorse) - An offline recommender system backend based on collaborative filtering written in Go.
*   [goscore (‚≠ê102)](https://github.com/asafschers/goscore) - Go Scoring API for PMML.
*   [gosseract (‚≠ê2.9k)](https://github.com/otiai10/gosseract) - Go package for OCR (Optical Character Recognition), by using Tesseract C++ library.

### Messaging

*   [ami (‚≠ê33)](https://github.com/kak-tus/ami) - Go client to reliable queues based on Redis Cluster Streams.
*   [amqp (‚≠ê1.8k)](https://github.com/rabbitmq/amqp091-go) - Go RabbitMQ Client Library.
*   [APNs2 (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/sideshow/apns2) - HTTP/2 Apple Push Notification provider for Go - Send push notifications to iOS, tvOS, Safari and OSX apps.
*   [Asynq (‚≠ê12k)](https://github.com/hibiken/asynq) - A simple, reliable, and efficient distributed task queue for Go built on top of Redis.
*   [Beaver (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/Clivern/Beaver) - A real time messaging server to build a scalable in-app notifications, multiplayer games, chat apps in web and mobile apps.
*   [Bus (‚≠ê349)](https://github.com/mustafaturan/bus) - Minimalist message bus implementation for internal communication.
*   [Centrifugo (‚≠ê9.1k)](https://github.com/centrifugal/centrifugo) - Real-time messaging (Websockets or SockJS) server in Go.
*   [Chanify (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/chanify/chanify) - A push notification server send message to your iOS devices.
*   [Commander (‚≠ê67)](https://github.com/jeroenrinzema/commander) - A high-level event driven consumer/producer supporting various "dialects" such as Apache Kafka.
*   [Confluent Kafka Golang Client (‚≠ê4.9k)](https://github.com/confluentinc/confluent-kafka-go) - confluent-kafka-go is Confluent's Golang client for Apache Kafka and the Confluent Platform.
*   [dbus (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/godbus/dbus) - Native Go bindings for D-Bus.
*   [drone-line (‚≠ê80)](https://github.com/appleboy/drone-line) - Sending [Line](https://at.line.me/en) notifications using a binary, docker or Drone CI.
*   [emitter (‚≠ê523)](https://github.com/olebedev/emitter) - Emits events using Go way, with wildcard, predicates, cancellation possibilities and many other good wins.
*   [event (‚≠ê59)](https://github.com/agoalofalife/event) - Implementation of the pattern observer.
*   [EventBus (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/asaskevich/EventBus) - The lightweight event bus with async compatibility.
*   [gaurun-client (‚≠ê11)](https://github.com/osamingo/gaurun-client) - Gaurun Client written in Go.
*   [Glue (‚≠ê420)](https://github.com/desertbit/glue) - Robust Go and Javascript Socket Library (Alternative to Socket.io).
*   [go-mq (‚≠ê90)](https://github.com/cheshir/go-mq) - RabbitMQ client with declarative configuration.
*   [go-notify (‚≠ê71)](https://github.com/TheCreeper/go-notify) - Native implementation of the freedesktop notification spec.
*   [go-nsq (‚≠ê2.6k)](https://github.com/nsqio/go-nsq) - the official Go package for NSQ.
*   [go-res (‚≠ê65)](https://github.com/jirenius/go-res) - Package for building REST/real-time services where clients are synchronized seamlessly, using NATS and Resgate.
*   [go-socket.io (‚≠ê5.8k)](https://github.com/googollee/go-socket.io) - socket.io library for golang, a realtime application framework.
*   [go-vitotrol (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/maxatome/go-vitotrol) - Client library to Viessmann Vitotrol web service.
*   [Gollum (‚≠ê941)](https://github.com/trivago/gollum) - A n:m multiplexer that gathers messages from different sources and broadcasts them to a set of destinations.
*   [golongpoll (‚≠ê663)](https://github.com/jcuga/golongpoll) - HTTP longpoll server library that makes web pub-sub simple.
*   [gopush-cluster (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/Terry-Mao/gopush-cluster) - gopush-cluster is a go push server cluster.
*   [gorush (‚≠ê8.4k)](https://github.com/appleboy/gorush) - Push notification server using [APNs2 (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/sideshow/apns2) and google [GCM (‚≠ê105)](https://github.com/google/go-gcm).
*   [gosd (‚≠ê26)](https://github.com/alexsniffin/gosd) - A library for scheduling when to dispatch a message to a channel.
*   [guble (‚≠ê160)](https://github.com/smancke/guble) - Messaging server using push notifications (Google Firebase Cloud Messaging, Apple Push Notification services, SMS) as well as websockets, a REST API, featuring distributed operation and message-persistence.
*   [hare (‚≠ê53)](https://github.com/leozz37/hare) - A user friendly library for sending messages and listening to TCP sockets.
*   [hub (‚≠ê147)](https://github.com/leandro-lugaresi/hub) - A Message/Event Hub for Go applications, using publish/subscribe pattern with support for alias like rabbitMQ exchanges.
*   [jazz (‚≠ê18)](https://github.com/socifi/jazz) - A simple RabbitMQ abstraction layer for queue administration and publishing and consuming of messages.
*   [machinery (‚≠ê7.8k)](https://github.com/RichardKnop/machinery) - Asynchronous task queue/job queue based on distributed message passing.
*   [mangos (‚≠ê715)](https://github.com/nanomsg/mangos) - Pure go implementation of the Nanomsg ("Scalability Protocols") with transport interoperability.
*   [melody (‚≠ê3.9k)](https://github.com/olahol/melody) - Minimalist framework for dealing with websocket sessions, includes broadcasting and automatic ping/pong handling.
*   [Mercure (‚≠ê5k)](https://github.com/dunglas/mercure) - Server and library to dispatch server-sent updates using the Mercure protocol (built on top of Server-Sent Events).
*   [messagebus (‚≠ê277)](https://github.com/vardius/message-bus) - messagebus is a Go simple async message bus, perfect for using as event bus when doing event sourcing, CQRS, DDD.
*   [nsq-event-bus (‚≠ê80)](https://github.com/rafaeljesus/nsq-event-bus) - A tiny wrapper around NSQ topic and channel.
*   [oplog (‚≠ê110)](https://github.com/dailymotion/oplog) - Generic oplog/replication system for REST APIs.
*   [pubsub (‚≠ê438)](https://github.com/tuxychandru/pubsub) - Simple pubsub package for go.
*   [rabbus (‚≠ê98)](https://github.com/rafaeljesus/rabbus) - A tiny wrapper over amqp exchanges and queues.
*   [rabtap (‚≠ê270)](https://github.com/jandelgado/rabtap) - RabbitMQ swiss army knife cli app.
*   [RapidMQ (‚≠ê69)](https://github.com/sybrexsys/RapidMQ) - RapidMQ is a lightweight and reliable library for managing of the local messages queue.
*   [redisqueue (‚≠ê134)](https://github.com/robinjoseph08/redisqueue) - redisqueue provides a producer and consumer of a queue that uses Redis streams.
*   [rmqconn (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/sbabiv/rmqconn) - RabbitMQ Reconnection. Wrapper over amqp.Connection and amqp.Dial. Allowing to do a reconnection when the connection is broken before forcing the call to the Close () method to be closed.
*   [sarama (‚≠ê12k)](https://github.com/Shopify/sarama) - Go library for Apache Kafka.
*   [Uniqush-Push (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/uniqush/uniqush-push) - Redis backed unified push service for server-side notifications to mobile devices.
*   [zmq4 (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/pebbe/zmq4) - Go interface to ZeroMQ version 4. Also available for [version 3 (‚≠ê133)](https://github.com/pebbe/zmq3) and [version 2 (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/pebbe/zmq2).

### Microsoft Office

*   [unioffice (‚≠ê4.6k)](https://github.com/unidoc/unioffice) - Pure go library for creating and processing Office Word (.docx), Excel (.xlsx) and Powerpoint (.pptx) documents.

Note: despite the org-name they do not represent official golang standards, see [this issue (‚≠ê53k)](https://github.com/golang-standards/project-layout/issues/117) for more information. Nonetheless, some may find the layout useful.

### Networking

*   [arp (‚≠ê375)](https://github.com/mdlayher/arp) - Package arp implements the ARP protocol, as described in RFC 826.

*   [dhcp6 (‚≠ê79)](https://github.com/mdlayher/dhcp6) - Package dhcp6 implements a DHCPv6 server, as described in RFC 3315.

*   [dnsmonster (‚≠ê332)](https://github.com/mosajjal/dnsmonster) - Passive DNS Capture/Monitoring Framework.

*   [ethernet (‚≠ê283)](https://github.com/mdlayher/ethernet) - Package ethernet implements marshaling and unmarshalling of IEEE 802.3 Ethernet II frames and IEEE 802.1Q VLAN tags.
*   [fasthttp (‚≠ê23k)](https://github.com/valyala/fasthttp) - Package fasthttp is a fast HTTP implementation for Go, up to 10 times faster than net/http.
*   [fortio (‚≠ê3.6k)](https://github.com/fortio/fortio) - Load testing library and command line tool, advanced echo server and web UI. Allows to specify a set query-per-second load and record latency histograms and other useful stats and graph them. Tcp, Http, gRPC.
*   [ftp (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/jlaffaye/ftp) - Package ftp implements a FTP client as described in [RFC 959](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc959).
*   [ftpserverlib (‚≠ê451)](https://github.com/fclairamb/ftpserverlib) - Fully featured FTP server library.
*   [gaio (‚≠ê794)](https://github.com/xtaci/gaio) - High performance async-io networking for Golang in proactor mode.
*   [gev (‚≠ê1.8k)](https://github.com/Allenxuxu/gev) - gev is a lightweight, fast non-blocking TCP network library based on Reactor mode.
*   [gmqtt (‚≠ê1k)](https://github.com/DrmagicE/gmqtt) - Gmqtt is a flexible, high-performance MQTT broker library that fully implements the MQTT protocol V3.1.1.
*   [gnet (‚≠ê11k)](https://github.com/panjf2000/gnet) - `gnet` is a high-performance, lightweight, non-blocking, event-driven networking framework written in pure Go.

*   [go-stun (‚≠ê709)](https://github.com/ccding/go-stun) - Go implementation of the STUN client (RFC 3489 and RFC 5389).
*   [gobgp (‚≠ê3.8k)](https://github.com/osrg/gobgp) - BGP implemented in the Go Programming Language.
*   [gopacket (‚≠ê6.6k)](https://github.com/google/gopacket) - Go library for packet processing with libpcap bindings.
*   [gopcap (‚≠ê491)](https://github.com/akrennmair/gopcap) - Go wrapper for libpcap.

*   [llb (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/kirillDanshin/llb) - It's a very simple but quick backend for proxy servers. Can be useful for fast redirection to predefined domain with zero memory allocation and fast response.
*   [mdns (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/hashicorp/mdns) - Simple mDNS (Multicast DNS) client/server library in Golang.

*   [nbio (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/lesismal/nbio) - Pure Go 1000k+ connections solution, support tls/http1.x/websocket and basically compatible with net/http, with high-performance and low memory cost, non-blocking, event-driven, easy-to-use.
*   [netpoll (‚≠ê4.4k)](https://github.com/cloudwego/netpoll) - A high-performance non-blocking I/O networking framework, which focused on RPC scenarios, developed by ByteDance.
*   [NFF-Go (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/intel-go/nff-go) - Framework for rapid development of performant network functions for cloud and bare-metal (former YANFF).
*   [peerdiscovery (‚≠ê659)](https://github.com/schollz/peerdiscovery) - Pure Go library for cross-platform local peer discovery using UDP multicast.
*   [portproxy (‚≠ê58)](https://github.com/aybabtme/portproxy) - Simple TCP proxy which adds CORS support to API's which don't support it.

*   [raw (‚≠ê425)](https://github.com/mdlayher/raw) - Package raw enables reading and writing data at the device driver level for a network interface.
*   [sftp (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/pkg/sftp) - Package sftp implements the SSH File Transfer Protocol as described in <https://filezilla-project.org/specs/draft-ietf-secsh-filexfer-02.txt>.
*   [ssh (‚≠ê3.9k)](https://github.com/gliderlabs/ssh) - Higher-level API for building SSH servers (wraps crypto/ssh).
*   [sslb (‚≠ê151)](https://github.com/eduardonunesp/sslb) - It's a Super Simples Load Balancer, just a little project to achieve some kind of performance.
*   [stun (‚≠ê494)](https://github.com/go-rtc/stun) - Go implementation of RFC 5389 STUN protocol.
*   [tspool (‚≠ê14)](https://github.com/two/tspool) - A TCP Library use worker pool to improve performance and protect your server.
*   [utp (‚≠ê178)](https://github.com/anacrolix/utp) - Go uTP micro transport protocol implementation.
*   [vssh (‚≠ê973)](https://github.com/yahoo/vssh) - Go library for building network and server automation over SSH protocol.
*   [water (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/songgao/water) - Simple TUN/TAP library.
*   [webrtc (‚≠ê15k)](https://github.com/pions/webrtc) - A pure Go implementation of the WebRTC API.
*   [winrm (‚≠ê444)](https://github.com/masterzen/winrm) - Go WinRM client to remotely execute commands on Windows machines.
*   [xtcp (‚≠ê157)](https://github.com/xfxdev/xtcp) - TCP Server Framework with simultaneous full duplex communication, graceful shutdown, and custom protocol.

### HTTP Clients

*   [gentleman (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/h2non/gentleman) - Full-featured plugin-driven HTTP client library.
*   [go-http-client (‚≠ê83)](https://github.com/bozd4g/go-http-client) - Make http calls simply and easily.
*   [go-req (‚≠ê22)](https://github.com/wenerme/go-req) - Declarative golang HTTP client.
*   [go-retryablehttp (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-retryablehttp) - Retryable HTTP client in Go.
*   [grequests (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/levigross/grequests) - A Go "clone" of the great and famous Requests library.
*   [heimdall (‚≠ê2.7k)](https://github.com/gojektech/heimdall) - An enhanced http client with retry and hystrix capabilities.
*   [httpretry (‚≠ê52)](https://github.com/ybbus/httpretry) - Enriches the default go HTTP client with retry functionality.
*   [pester (‚≠ê652)](https://github.com/sethgrid/pester) - Go HTTP client calls with retries, backoff, and concurrency.
*   [request (‚≠ê292)](https://github.com/monaco-io/request) - HTTP client for golang. If you have experience about axios or requests, you will love it. No 3rd dependency.
*   [requests (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/carlmjohnson/requests) - HTTP requests for Gophers. Uses context.Context and doesn't hide the underlying net/http.Client, making it compatible with standard Go APIs. Also includes testing tools.
*   [resty (‚≠ê11k)](https://github.com/go-resty/resty) - Simple HTTP and REST client for Go inspired by Ruby rest-client.
*   [rq (‚≠ê53)](https://github.com/ddo/rq) - A nicer interface for golang stdlib HTTP client.
*   [sling (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/dghubble/sling) - Sling is a Go HTTP client library for creating and sending API requests.

### OpenGL

*   [gl (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/go-gl/gl) - Go bindings for OpenGL (generated via glow).
*   [glfw (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/go-gl/glfw) - Go bindings for GLFW 3.

*   [goxjs/glfw (‚≠ê83)](https://github.com/goxjs/glfw) - Go cross-platform glfw library for creating an OpenGL context and receiving events.
*   [mathgl (‚≠ê580)](https://github.com/go-gl/mathgl) - Pure Go math package specialized for 3D math, with inspiration from GLM.

### ORM

*   [cacheme (‚≠ê24)](https://github.com/Yiling-J/cacheme-go) - Schema based, typed Redis caching/memoize framework for Go.
*   [ent (‚≠ê16k)](https://github.com/facebook/ent) - An entity framework for Go. Simple, yet powerful ORM for modeling and querying data.
*   [go-firestorm (‚≠ê52)](https://github.com/jschoedt/go-firestorm) - A simple ORM for Google/Firebase Cloud Firestore.
*   [go-sql (‚≠ê180)](https://github.com/rushteam/gosql) - A easy ORM for mysql.
*   [go-sqlbuilder (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/huandu/go-sqlbuilder) - A flexible and powerful SQL string builder library plus a zero-config ORM.
*   [go-store (‚≠ê113)](https://github.com/gosuri/go-store) - Simple and fast Redis backed key-value store library for Go.
*   [GORM (‚≠ê39k)](https://github.com/go-gorm/gorm) - The fantastic ORM library for Golang, aims to be developer friendly.
*   [gormt (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/xxjwxc/gormt) - Mysql database to golang gorm struct.
*   [gorp (‚≠ê3.7k)](https://github.com/go-gorp/gorp) - Go Relational Persistence, ORM-ish library for Go.
*   [grimoire (‚≠ê163)](https://github.com/Fs02/grimoire) - Grimoire is a database access layer and validation for golang. (Support: MySQL, PostgreSQL and SQLite3).
*   [lore (‚≠ê14)](https://github.com/abrahambotros/lore) - Simple and lightweight pseudo-ORM/pseudo-struct-mapping environment for Go.
*   [marlow (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/marlow/marlow) - Generated ORM from project structs for compile time safety assurances.
*   [pop/soda (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/gobuffalo/pop) - Database migration, creation, ORM, etc... for MySQL, PostgreSQL, and SQLite.
*   [Prisma (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/prisma/prisma-client-go) - Prisma Client Go, Typesafe database access for Go.
*   [reform (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/go-reform/reform) - Better ORM for Go, based on non-empty interfaces and code generation.
*   [rel (‚≠ê783)](https://github.com/go-rel/rel) - Modern Database Access Layer for Golang - Testable, Extendable and Crafted Into a Clean and Elegant API.
*   [SQLBoiler (‚≠ê6.9k)](https://github.com/volatiletech/sqlboiler) - ORM generator. Generate a featureful and blazing-fast ORM tailored to your database schema.
*   [upper.io/db (‚≠ê3.6k)](https://github.com/upper/db) - Single interface for interacting with different data sources through the use of adapters that wrap mature database drivers.
*   [XORM](https://gitea.com/xorm/xorm) - Simple and powerful ORM for Go. (Support: MySQL, MyMysql, PostgreSQL, Tidb, SQLite3, MsSql and Oracle).
*   [Zoom (‚≠ê312)](https://github.com/albrow/zoom) - Blazing-fast datastore and querying engine built on Redis.

### Package Management

*   [go modules](https://golang.org/cmd/go/#hdr-Modules__module_versions__and_more) - Modules are the unit of source code interchange and versioning. The go command has direct support for working with modules, including recording and resolving dependencies on other modules.
*   [glide (‚≠ê8.1k)](https://github.com/Masterminds/glide) - Manage your golang vendor and vendored packages with ease. Inspired by tools like Maven, Bundler, and Pip.
*   [godep (‚≠ê5.5k)](https://github.com/tools/godep) - dependency tool for go, godep helps build packages reproducibly by fixing their dependencies.
*   [goop (‚≠ê775)](https://github.com/nitrous-io/goop) - Simple dependency manager for Go (golang), inspired by Bundler.
*   [gop (‚≠ê48)](https://github.com/lunny/gop) - Build and manage your Go applications out of GOPATH.
*   [gopm (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/gpmgo/gopm) - Go Package Manager.
*   [govendor (‚≠ê4.9k)](https://github.com/kardianos/govendor) - Go Package Manager. Go vendor tool that works with the standard vendor file.
*   [gpm (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/pote/gpm) - Barebones dependency manager for Go.
*   [johnny-deps (‚≠ê213)](https://github.com/VividCortex/johnny-deps) - Minimal dependency version using Git.
*   [modgv (‚≠ê492)](https://github.com/lucasepe/modgv) - Converts 'go mod graph' output into Graphviz's DOT language.
*   [mvn-golang (‚≠ê165)](https://github.com/raydac/mvn-golang) - plugin that provides way for auto-loading of Golang SDK, dependency management and start build environment in Maven project infrastructure.
*   [VenGO (‚≠ê126)](https://github.com/DamnWidget/VenGO) - create and manage exportable isolated go virtual environments.

### Science and Data Analysis

*   [chart (‚≠ê773)](https://github.com/vdobler/chart) - Simple Chart Plotting library for Go. Supports many graphs types.
*   [dataframe-go (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/rocketlaunchr/dataframe-go) - Dataframes for machine-learning and statistics (similar to pandas).
