*   [evaler (‚≠ê51)](https://github.com/soniah/evaler) - Simple floating point arithmetic expression evaluator.
*   [ewma (‚≠ê448)](https://github.com/VividCortex/ewma) - Exponentially-weighted moving averages.
*   [geom (‚≠ê55)](https://github.com/skelterjohn/geom) - 2D geometry for golang.
*   [go-dsp (‚≠ê882)](https://github.com/mjibson/go-dsp) - Digital Signal Processing for Go.
*   [go-estimate (‚≠ê117)](https://github.com/milosgajdos/go-estimate) - State estimation and filtering algorithms in Go.
*   [go-gt (‚≠ê11)](https://github.com/ThePaw/go-gt) - Graph theory algorithms written in "Go" language.
*   [godesim (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/soypat/godesim) - Extended/multivariable ODE solver framework for event-based simulations with simple API.
*   [goent (‚≠ê35)](https://github.com/kzahedi/goent) - GO Implementation of Entropy Measures.
*   [gonum (‚≠ê8.1k)](https://github.com/gonum/gonum) - Gonum is a set of numeric libraries for the Go programming language. It contains libraries for matrices, statistics, optimization, and more.
*   [gonum/plot (‚≠ê2.9k)](https://github.com/gonum/plot) - gonum/plot provides an API for building and drawing plots in Go.
*   [goraph (‚≠ê743)](https://github.com/gyuho/goraph) - Pure Go graph theory library(data structure, algorithm visualization).
*   [gosl (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/cpmech/gosl) - Go scientific library for linear algebra, FFT, geometry, NURBS, numerical methods, probabilities, optimisation, differential equations, and more.
*   [GoStats (‚≠ê22)](https://github.com/OGFris/GoStats) - GoStats is an Open Source GoLang library for math statistics mostly used in Machine Learning domains, it covers most of the Statistical measures functions.
*   [graph (‚≠ê730)](https://github.com/yourbasic/graph) - Library of basic graph algorithms.
*   [jsonl-graph (‚≠ê75)](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/jsonl-graph) - Tool to manipulate JSONL graphs with graphviz support.
*   [ode (‚≠ê22)](https://github.com/ChristopherRabotin/ode) - Ordinary differential equation (ODE) solver which supports extended states and channel-based iteration stop conditions.
*   [orb (‚≠ê1k)](https://github.com/paulmach/orb) - 2D geometry types with clipping, GeoJSON and Mapbox Vector Tile support.
*   [pagerank (‚≠ê86)](https://github.com/alixaxel/pagerank) - Weighted PageRank algorithm implemented in Go.
*   [piecewiselinear (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/sgreben/piecewiselinear) - Tiny linear interpolation library.
*   [PiHex (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/claygod/PiHex) - Implementation of the "Bailey-Borwein-Plouffe" algorithm for the hexadecimal number Pi.
*   [rootfinding (‚≠ê11)](https://github.com/khezen/rootfinding) - root-finding algorithms library for finding roots of quadratic functions.
*   [sparse (‚≠ê165)](https://github.com/james-bowman/sparse) - Go Sparse matrix formats for linear algebra supporting scientific and machine learning applications, compatible with gonum matrix libraries.
*   [stats (‚≠ê3k)](https://github.com/montanaflynn/stats) - Statistics package with common functions missing from the Golang standard library.
*   [streamtools (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/nytlabs/streamtools) - general purpose, graphical tool for dealing with streams of data.
*   [TextRank (‚≠ê217)](https://github.com/DavidBelicza/TextRank) - TextRank implementation in Golang with extendable features (summarization, weighting, phrase extraction) and multithreading (goroutine) support.
*   [triangolatte (‚≠ê36)](https://github.com/tchayen/triangolatte) - 2D triangulation library. Allows translating lines and polygons (both based on points) to the language of GPUs.

### Security

*   [acmetool (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/hlandau/acme) - ACME (Let's Encrypt) client tool with automatic renewal.
*   [acra (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/cossacklabs/acra) - Network encryption proxy to protect database-based applications from data leaks: strong selective encryption, SQL injections prevention, intrusion detection system.
*   [age (‚≠ê19k)](https://github.com/FiloSottile/age) - A simple, modern and secure encryption tool (and Go library) with small explicit keys, no config options, and UNIX-style composability.
*   [argon2-hashing (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/andskur/argon2-hashing) - light wrapper around Go's argon2 package that closely mirrors with Go's standard library Bcrypt and simple-scrypt package.
*   [argon2pw (‚≠ê91)](https://github.com/raja/argon2pw) - Argon2 password hash generation with constant-time password comparison.
*   [BadActor (‚≠ê324)](https://github.com/jaredfolkins/badactor) - In-memory, application-driven jailer built in the spirit of fail2ban.
*   [Cameradar (‚≠ê4.5k)](https://github.com/Ullaakut/cameradar) - Tool and library to remotely hack RTSP streams from surveillance cameras.
*   [certificates (‚≠ê38)](https://github.com/mvmaasakkers/certificates) - An opinionated tool for generating tls certificates.
*   [CertMagic (‚≠ê5.3k)](https://github.com/caddyserver/certmagic) - Mature, robust, and powerful ACME client integration for fully-managed TLS certificate issuance and renewal.
*   [dongle (‚≠ê988)](https://github.com/golang-module/dongle) - A simple, semantic and developer-friendly golang package for encoding\&decoding and encryption\&decryption.
*   [firewalld-rest (‚≠ê342)](https://github.com/prashantgupta24/firewalld-rest) - A rest application to dynamically update firewalld rules on a linux server.
*   [go-generate-password (‚≠ê55)](https://github.com/m1/go-generate-password) - Password generator that can be used on the cli or as a library.
*   [go-htpasswd (‚≠ê44)](https://github.com/tg123/go-htpasswd) - Apache htpasswd Parser for Go.
*   [go-password-validator (‚≠ê538)](https://github.com/lane-c-wagner/go-password-validator) - Password validator based on raw cryptographic entropy values.
*   [go-yara (‚≠ê373)](https://github.com/hillu/go-yara) - Go Bindings for [YARA (‚≠ê139)](https://github.com/plusvic/yara), the "pattern matching swiss knife for malware researchers (and everyone else)".
*   [goArgonPass (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/dwin/goArgonPass) - Argon2 password hash and verification designed to be compatible with existing Python and PHP implementations.
*   [goSecretBoxPassword (‚≠ê60)](https://github.com/dwin/goSecretBoxPassword) - A probably paranoid package for securely hashing and encrypting passwords.
*   [lego (‚≠ê8.7k)](https://github.com/go-acme/lego) - Pure Go ACME client library and CLI tool (for use with Let's Encrypt).
*   [memguard (‚≠ê2.6k)](https://github.com/awnumar/memguard) - A pure Go library for handling sensitive values in memory.
*   [nacl (‚≠ê548)](https://github.com/kevinburke/nacl) - Go implementation of the NaCL set of API's.
*   [optimus-go (‚≠ê362)](https://github.com/pjebs/optimus-go) - ID hashing and Obfuscation using Knuth's Algorithm.
*   [passlib (‚≠ê293)](https://github.com/hlandau/passlib) - Futureproof password hashing library.
*   [secure (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/unrolled/secure) - HTTP middleware for Go that facilitates some quick security wins.
*   [secureio (‚≠ê34)](https://github.com/xaionaro-go/secureio) - An keyexchanging+authenticating+encrypting wrapper and multiplexer for `io.ReadWriteCloser` based on XChaCha20-poly1305, ECDH and ED25519.
*   [simple-scrypt (‚≠ê201)](https://github.com/elithrar/simple-scrypt) - Scrypt package with a simple, obvious API and automatic cost calibration built-in.
*   [ssh-vault (‚≠ê472)](https://github.com/ssh-vault/ssh-vault) - encrypt/decrypt using ssh keys.
*   [sslmgr (‚≠ê30)](https://github.com/adrianosela/sslmgr) - SSL certificates made easy with a high level wrapper around acme/autocert.
*   [themis (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/cossacklabs/themis) - high-level cryptographic library for solving typical data security tasks (secure data storage, secure messaging, zero-knowledge proof authentication), available for 14 languages, best fit for multi-platform apps.

### Serialization

*   [bambam (‚≠ê65)](https://github.com/glycerine/bambam) - generator for Cap'n Proto schemas from go.

*   [cbor (‚≠ê896)](https://github.com/fxamacker/cbor) - Small, safe, and easy CBOR encoding and decoding library.
*   [colfer (‚≠ê749)](https://github.com/pascaldekloe/colfer) - Code generation for the Colfer binary format.
*   [csvutil (‚≠ê995)](https://github.com/jszwec/csvutil) - High Performance, idiomatic CSV record encoding and decoding to native Go structures.
*   [elastic (‚≠ê25)](https://github.com/epiclabs-io/elastic) - Convert slices, maps or any other unknown value across different types at run-time, no matter what.
*   [fixedwidth (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/huydang284/fixedwidth) - Fixed-width text formatting (UTF-8 supported).
*   [fwencoder (‚≠ê27)](https://github.com/o1egl/fwencoder) - Fixed width file parser (encoding and decoding library) for Go.
*   [go-capnproto (‚≠ê288)](https://github.com/glycerine/go-capnproto) - Cap'n Proto library and parser for go.
*   [go-codec (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/ugorji/go) - High Performance, feature-Rich, idiomatic encode, decode and rpc library for msgpack, cbor and json, with runtime-based OR code-generation support.
*   [gogoprotobuf (‚≠ê5.7k)](https://github.com/gogo/protobuf) - Protocol Buffers for Go with Gadgets.
*   [goprotobuf (‚≠ê10k)](https://github.com/golang/protobuf) - Go support, in the form of a library and protocol compiler plugin, for Google's protocol buffers.
*   [jsoniter (‚≠ê14k)](https://github.com/json-iterator/go) - High-performance 100% compatible drop-in replacement of "encoding/json".
*   [mapstructure (‚≠ê8k)](https://github.com/mitchellh/mapstructure) - Go library for decoding generic map values into native Go structures.
*   [php\_session\_decoder (‚≠ê167)](https://github.com/yvasiyarov/php_session_decoder) - GoLang library for working with PHP session format and PHP Serialize/Unserialize functions.
*   [pletter (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/vimeda/pletter) - A standard way to wrap a proto message for message brokers.
*   [structomap (‚≠ê144)](https://github.com/tuvistavie/structomap) - Library to easily and dynamically generate maps from static structures.
*   [unitpacking (‚≠ê7)](https://github.com/recolude/unitpacking) - Library to pack unit vectors into as fewest bytes as possible.

### Server Applications

*   [algernon (‚≠ê2.9k)](https://github.com/xyproto/algernon) - HTTP/2 web server with built-in support for Lua, Markdown, GCSS and Amber.
*   [Caddy (‚≠ê65k)](https://github.com/caddyserver/caddy) - Caddy is an alternative, HTTP/2 web server that's easy to configure and use.

*   [cortex-tenant (‚≠ê125)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/cortex-tenant) - Prometheus remote write proxy that adds add Cortex tenant ID header based on metric labels.
*   [devd (‚≠ê3.5k)](https://github.com/cortesi/devd) - Local webserver for developers.
*   [discovery (‚≠ê1.8k)](https://github.com/Bilibili/discovery) - A registry for resilient mid-tier load balancing and failover.
*   [dudeldu (‚≠ê145)](https://github.com/krotik/dudeldu) - A simple SHOUTcast server.
*   [Easegress (‚≠ê5.8k)](https://github.com/megaease/easegress) - A cloud native high availability/performance traffic orchestration system with observability and extensibility.
*   [Euterpe (‚≠ê556)](https://github.com/ironsmile/euterpe) - Self-hosted music streaming server with built-in web UI and REST API.
*   [Fider (‚≠ê3.6k)](https://github.com/getfider/fider) - Fider is an open platform to collect and organize customer feedback.
*   [Flagr (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/checkr/flagr) - Flagr is an open-source feature flagging and A/B testing service.
*   [flipt (‚≠ê4.5k)](https://github.com/markphelps/flipt) - A self contained feature flag solution written in Go and Vue.js
*   [go-feature-flag (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/thomaspoignant/go-feature-flag) - A simple, complete and lightweight self-hosted feature flag solution 100% Open Source.
*   [go-proxy-cache (‚≠ê143)](https://github.com/fabiocicerchia/go-proxy-cache) - Simple Reverse Proxy with Caching, written in Go, using Redis.
*   [lets-proxy2 (‚≠ê100)](https://github.com/rekby/lets-proxy2) - Reverse proxy for handle https with issue certificates in fly from lets-encrypt.
*   [minio (‚≠ê54k)](https://github.com/minio/minio) - Minio is a distributed object storage server.
*   [Moxy (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/sinhashubham95/moxy) - Moxy is a simple mocker and proxy application server, you can create mock endpoints as well as proxy requests in case no mock exists for the endpoint.
*   [nginx-prometheus (‚≠ê41)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/nginx-prometheus) - Nginx log parser and exporter to Prometheus.
*   [nsq](https://nsq.io/) - A realtime distributed messaging platform.
*   [protoxy (‚≠ê35)](https://github.com/camgraff/protoxy) - A proxy server that converts JSON request bodies to Protocol Buffers.
*   [psql-streamer (‚≠ê60)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/psql-streamer) - Stream database events from PostgreSQL to Kafka.
*   [riemann-relay (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/riemann-relay) - Relay to load-balance Riemann events and/or convert them to Carbon.
*   [RoadRunner (‚≠ê8.2k)](https://github.com/spiral/roadrunner) - High-performance PHP application server, load-balancer and process manager.
*   [SFTPGo (‚≠ê11k)](https://github.com/drakkan/sftpgo) - Fully featured and highly configurable SFTP server with optional FTP/S and WebDAV support. It can serve local filesystem and Cloud Storage backends such as S3 and Google Cloud Storage.
*   [Trickster (‚≠ê2k)](https://github.com/tricksterproxy/trickster) - HTTP reverse proxy cache and time series accelerator.

### Stream Processing

*   [go-streams (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/reugn/go-streams) - Go stream processing library.
*   [machine (‚≠ê162)](https://github.com/whitaker-io/machine) - Go library for writing and generating stream workers with built in metrics and traceability.
*   [stream (‚≠ê95)](https://github.com/youthlin/stream) - Go Stream, like Java 8 Stream: Filter/Map/FlatMap/Peek/Sorted/ForEach/Reduce...

### Template Engines

*   [ego (‚≠ê584)](https://github.com/benbjohnson/ego) - Lightweight templating language that lets you write templates in Go. Templates are translated into Go and compiled.
*   [fasttemplate (‚≠ê876)](https://github.com/valyala/fasttemplate) - Simple and fast template engine. Substitutes template placeholders up to 10x faster than [text/template](https://golang.org/pkg/text/template/).
*   [goview (‚≠ê455)](https://github.com/foolin/goview) - Goview is a lightweight, minimalist and idiomatic template library based on golang html/template for building Go web application.
*   [jet (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/CloudyKit/jet) - Jet template engine.
*   [liquid (‚≠ê309)](https://github.com/osteele/liquid) - Go implementation of Shopify Liquid templates.
*   [maroto (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/johnfercher/maroto) - A maroto way to create PDFs. Maroto is inspired in Bootstrap and uses gofpdf. Fast and simple.
*   [pongo2 (‚≠ê3k)](https://github.com/flosch/pongo2) - Django-like template-engine for Go.
*   [quicktemplate (‚≠ê3.2k)](https://github.com/valyala/quicktemplate) - Fast, powerful, yet easy to use template engine. Converts templates into Go code and then compiles it.
*   [raymond (‚≠ê638)](https://github.com/aymerick/raymond) - Complete handlebars implementation in Go.
*   [Razor (‚≠ê872)](https://github.com/sipin/gorazor) - Razor view engine for Golang.
*   [Soy (‚≠ê175)](https://github.com/robfig/soy) - Closure templates (aka Soy templates) for Go, following the [official spec](https://developers.google.com/closure/templates/).
*   [tbd (‚≠ê27)](https://github.com/lucasepe/tbd) - A really simple way to create text templates with placeholders - exposes extra builtin Git repo metadata.

### Testing Frameworks

*   [apitest](https://apitest.dev) - Simple and extensible behavioural testing library for REST based services or HTTP handlers that supports mocking external http calls and rendering of sequence diagrams.

### Mock

*   [counterfeiter (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/maxbrunsfeld/counterfeiter) - Tool for generating self-contained mock objects.

### Fuzzing and delta-debugging/reducing/shrinking

*   [go-fuzz (‚≠ê4.8k)](https://github.com/dvyukov/go-fuzz) - Randomized testing system.

### Selenium and browser control tools

*   [cdp (‚≠ê756)](https://github.com/mafredri/cdp) - Type-safe bindings for the Chrome Debugging Protocol that can be used with browsers or other debug targets that implement it.

### Fail injection

*   [failpoint (‚≠ê852)](https://github.com/pingcap/failpoint) - An implementation of [failpoints](https://www.freebsd.org/cgi/man.cgi?query=fail) for Golang.

### UUID

*   [goid (‚≠ê41)](https://github.com/jakehl/goid) - Generate and Parse RFC4122 compliant V4 UUIDs.
*   [gouid (‚≠ê26)](https://github.com/twharmon/gouid) - Generate cryptographically secure random string IDs with just one allocation.
*   [nanoid (‚≠ê62)](https://github.com/aidarkhanov/nanoid) - A tiny and efficient Go unique string ID generator.
*   [sno (‚≠ê91)](https://github.com/muyo/sno) - Compact, sortable and fast unique IDs with embedded metadata.
*   [ulid (‚≠ê4.8k)](https://github.com/oklog/ulid) - Go implementation of ULID (Universally Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifier).
*   [uniq](https://gitlab.com/skilstak/code/go/uniq) - No hassle safe, fast unique identifiers with commands.
*   [uuid (‚≠ê18)](https://github.com/agext/uuid) - Generate, encode, and decode UUIDs v1 with fast or cryptographic-quality random node identifier.
*   [uuid (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/gofrs/uuid) - Implementation of Universally Unique Identifier (UUID). Supports both creation and parsing of UUIDs. Actively maintained fork of satori uuid.
*   [uuid (‚≠ê5.7k)](https://github.com/google/uuid) - Go package for UUIDs based on RFC 4122 and DCE 1.1: Authentication and Security Services.
*   [wuid (‚≠ê540)](https://github.com/edwingeng/wuid) - An extremely fast globally unique number generator.
*   [xid (‚≠ê4.2k)](https://github.com/rs/xid) - Xid is a globally unique id generator library, ready to be safely used directly in your server code.

### Validation

*   [checkdigit (‚≠ê111)](https://github.com/osamingo/checkdigit) - Provide check digit algorithms (Luhn, Verhoeff, Damm) and calculators (ISBN, EAN, JAN, UPC, etc.).
*   [gody (‚≠ê157)](https://github.com/guiferpa/gody) - :balloon: A lightweight struct validator for Go.
*   [govalid (‚≠ê98)](https://github.com/twharmon/govalid) - Fast, tag-based validation for structs.
*   [govalidator (‚≠ê6.2k)](https://github.com/asaskevich/govalidator) - Validators and sanitizers for strings, numerics, slices and structs.
*   [govalidator (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/thedevsaddam/govalidator) - Validate Golang request data with simple rules. Highly inspired by Laravel's request validation.
*   [jio (‚≠ê118)](https://github.com/faceair/jio) - jio is a json schema validator similar to [joi (‚≠ê21k)](https://github.com/hapijs/joi).
*   [ozzo-validation (‚≠ê4k)](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-validation) - Supports validation of various data types (structs, strings, maps, slices, etc.) with configurable and extensible validation rules specified in usual code constructs instead of struct tags.
*   [validate (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/gookit/validate) - Go package for data validation and filtering. support validate Map, Struct, Request(Form, JSON, url.Values, Uploaded Files) data and more features.
*   [validate (‚≠ê93)](https://github.com/gobuffalo/validate) - This package provides a framework for writing validations for Go applications.
*   [validator (‚≠ê19k)](https://github.com/go-playground/validator) - Go Struct and Field validation, including Cross Field, Cross Struct, Map, Slice and Array diving.

### Middlewares / Actual middlewares

*   [client-timing (‚≠ê24)](https://github.com/posener/client-timing) - An HTTP client for Server-Timing header.
*   [CORS (‚≠ê2.8k)](https://github.com/rs/cors) - Easily add CORS capabilities to your API.
*   [formjson (‚≠ê38)](https://github.com/rs/formjson) - Transparently handle JSON input as a standard form POST.
*   [go-fault (‚≠ê509)](https://github.com/github/go-fault) - Fault injection middleware for Go.
*   [go-server-timing (‚≠ê859)](https://github.com/mitchellh/go-server-timing) - Add/parse Server-Timing header.
*   [Limiter (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/ulule/limiter) - Dead simple rate limit middleware for Go.
*   [ln-paywall (‚≠ê155)](https://github.com/philippgille/ln-paywall) - Go middleware for monetizing APIs on a per-request basis with the Lightning Network (Bitcoin).
*   [mid (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/bobg/mid) - Miscellaneous HTTP middleware features: idiomatic error return from handlers; receive/respond with JSON data; request tracing; and more.
*   [rk-gin (‚≠ê50)](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-gin) - Middleware for Gin framework with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
*   [rk-grpc (‚≠ê77)](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-grpc) - Middleware for gRPC with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
*   [Tollbooth (‚≠ê2.8k)](https://github.com/didip/tollbooth) - Rate limit HTTP request handler.
*   [XFF (‚≠ê100)](https://github.com/sebest/xff) - Handle `X-Forwarded-For` header and friends.

### Middlewares / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [alice (‚≠ê3.3k)](https://github.com/justinas/alice) - Painless middleware chaining for Go.
*   [catena (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/codemodus/catena) - http.Handler wrapper catenation (same API as "chain").
*   [chain (‚≠ê61)](https://github.com/codemodus/chain) - Handler wrapper chaining with scoped data (net/context-based "middleware").
*   [gores (‚≠ê106)](https://github.com/alioygur/gores) - Go package that handles HTML, JSON, XML and etc. responses. Useful for RESTful APIs.
*   [interpose (‚≠ê293)](https://github.com/carbocation/interpose) - Minimalist net/http middleware for golang.
*   [mediary (‚≠ê88)](https://github.com/HereMobilityDevelopers/mediary) - add interceptors to `http.Client` to allow dumping/shaping/tracing/... of requests/responses.
*   [muxchain (‚≠ê206)](https://github.com/stephens2424/muxchain) - Lightweight middleware for net/http.
*   [negroni (‚≠ê7.5k)](https://github.com/urfave/negroni) - Idiomatic HTTP middleware for Golang.
*   [render (‚≠ê2k)](https://github.com/unrolled/render) - Go package for easily rendering JSON, XML, and HTML template responses.
*   [renderer (‚≠ê262)](https://github.com/thedevsaddam/renderer) - Simple, lightweight and faster response (JSON, JSONP, XML, YAML, HTML, File) rendering package for Go.
*   [rye (‚≠ê100)](https://github.com/InVisionApp/rye) - Tiny Go middleware library (with canned Middlewares) that supports JWT, CORS, Statsd, and Go 1.7 context.
*   [stats (‚≠ê593)](https://github.com/thoas/stats) - Go middleware that stores various information about your web application.

### Routers / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [alien (‚≠ê134)](https://github.com/gernest/alien) - Lightweight and fast http router from outer space.
*   [bellt (‚≠ê54)](https://github.com/GuilhermeCaruso/bellt) - A simple Go HTTP router.
*   [Bone (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/go-zoo/bone) - Lightning Fast HTTP Multiplexer.
*   [Bxog (‚≠ê101)](https://github.com/claygod/Bxog) - Simple and fast HTTP router for Go. It works with routes of varying difficulty, length and nesting. And he knows how to create a URL from the received parameters.
*   [chi (‚≠ê20k)](https://github.com/go-chi/chi) - Small, fast and expressive HTTP router built on net/context.
*   [fasthttprouter (‚≠ê871)](https://github.com/buaazp/fasthttprouter) - High performance router forked from `httprouter`. The first router fit for `fasthttp`.
*   [FastRouter (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/razonyang/fastrouter) - a fast, flexible HTTP router written in Go.
*   [gocraft/web (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/gocraft/web) - Mux and middleware package in Go.
*   [Goji (‚≠ê971)](https://github.com/goji/goji) - Goji is a minimalistic and flexible HTTP request multiplexer with support for `net/context`.
*   [goroute (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/goroute/route) - Simple yet powerful HTTP request multiplexer.
*   [GoRouter (‚≠ê153)](https://github.com/vardius/gorouter) - GoRouter is a Server/API micro framework, HTTP request router, multiplexer, mux that provides request router with middleware supporting `net/context`.
*   [gowww/router (‚≠ê185)](https://github.com/gowww/router) - Lightning fast HTTP router fully compatible with the net/http.Handler interface.
*   [httprouter (‚≠ê17k)](https://github.com/julienschmidt/httprouter) - High performance router. Use this and the standard http handlers to form a very high performance web framework.
*   [httptreemux (‚≠ê619)](https://github.com/dimfeld/httptreemux) - High-speed, flexible tree-based HTTP router for Go. Inspiration from httprouter.
*   [lars (‚≠ê384)](https://github.com/go-playground/lars) - Is a lightweight, fast and extensible zero allocation HTTP router for Go used to create customizable frameworks.
*   [mux (‚≠ê21k)](https://github.com/gorilla/mux) - Powerful URL router and dispatcher for golang.
*   [ngamux (‚≠ê71)](https://github.com/ngamux/ngamux) - Simple HTTP router for Go.
*   [ozzo-routing (‚≠ê456)](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-routing) - An extremely fast Go (golang) HTTP router that supports regular expression route matching. Comes with full support for building RESTful APIs.
*   [pure (‚≠ê150)](https://github.com/go-playground/pure) - Is a lightweight HTTP router that sticks to the std "net/http" implementation.
*   [Siesta (‚≠ê348)](https://github.com/VividCortex/siesta) - Composable framework to write middleware and handlers.
*   [vestigo (‚≠ê267)](https://github.com/husobee/vestigo) - Performant, stand-alone, HTTP compliant URL Router for go web applications.
*   [violetear (‚≠ê107)](https://github.com/nbari/violetear) - Go HTTP router.
*   [xmux (‚≠ê99)](https://github.com/rs/xmux) - High performance muxer based on `httprouter` with `net/context` support.

*   [Guora (‚≠ê674)](https://github.com/meloalright/guora) - A self-hosted Quora like web application written in Go.
*   [hoofli (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/dnnrly/hoofli) - Generate PlantUML diagrams from Chrome or Firefox network inspections.
*   [hugo](https://gohugo.io/) - Fast and Modern Static Website Engine.
*   [ide (‚≠ê361)](https://github.com/thestrukture/ide) - Browser accessible IDE. Designed for Go with Go.
*   [joincap (‚≠ê217)](https://github.com/assafmo/joincap) - Command-line utility for merging multiple pcap files together.
*   [Juju](https://jujucharms.com/) - Cloud-agnostic service deployment and orchestration - supports EC2, Azure, Openstack, MAAS and more.
*   [Leaps (‚≠ê756)](https://github.com/jeffail/leaps) - Pair programming service using Operational Transforms.
*   [lgo (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/yunabe/lgo) - Interactive Go programming with Jupyter. It supports code completion, code inspection and 100% Go compatibility.
*   [limetext](https://limetext.github.io) - Lime Text is a powerful and elegant text editor primarily developed in Go that aims to be a Free and open-source software successor to Sublime Text.
*   [LiteIDE (‚≠ê7.7k)](https://github.com/visualfc/liteide) - LiteIDE is a simple, open source, cross-platform Go IDE.
*   [mockingjay (‚≠ê564)](https://github.com/quii/mockingjay-server) - Fake HTTP servers and consumer driven contracts from one configuration file. You can also make the server randomly misbehave to help do more realistic performance tests.
*   [myLG (‚≠ê2.7k)](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/mylg) - Command Line Network Diagnostic tool written in Go.
*   [naclpipe (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/unix4fun/naclpipe) - Simple NaCL EC25519 based crypto pipe tool written in Go.
*   [Neo-cowsay (‚≠ê328)](https://github.com/Code-Hex/Neo-cowsay) - üêÆ cowsay is reborn. for a New Era.
*   [nes (‚≠ê5.6k)](https://github.com/fogleman/nes) - Nintendo Entertainment System (NES) emulator written in Go.
*   [Orbit (‚≠ê186)](https://github.com/gulien/orbit) - A simple tool for running commands and generating files from templates.
*   [peg (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/pointlander/peg) - Peg, Parsing Expression Grammar, is an implementation of a Packrat parser generator.
*   [Plik (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/root-gg/plik) - Plik is a temporary file upload system (Wetransfer like) in Go.
*   [restic (‚≠ê29k)](https://github.com/restic/restic) - De-duplicating backup program.
*   [scc (‚≠ê7.5k)](https://github.com/boyter/scc) - Sloc Cloc and Code, a very fast accurate code counter with complexity calculations and COCOMO estimates.
*   [Seaweed File System (‚≠ê25k)](https://github.com/chrislusf/seaweedfs) - Fast, Simple and Scalable Distributed File System with O(1) disk seek.
*   [shell2http (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/msoap/shell2http) - Executing shell commands via http server (for prototyping or remote control).
*   [Snitch (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/lucasgomide/snitch) - Simple way to notify your team and many tools when someone has deployed any application via Tsuru.
*   [Stack Up (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/pressly/sup) - Stack Up, a super simple deployment tool - just Unix - think of it like 'make' for a network of servers.
*   [syncthing](https://syncthing.net/) - Open, decentralized file synchronization tool and protocol.
*   [tcpdog (‚≠ê260)](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/tcpdog) - eBPF based TCP observability.
*   [toxiproxy (‚≠ê11k)](https://github.com/shopify/toxiproxy) - Proxy to simulate network and system conditions for automated tests.
*   [tsuru](https://tsuru.io/) - Extensible and open source Platform as a Service software.
*   [vaku (‚≠ê155)](https://github.com/lingrino/vaku) - CLI & API for folder-based functions in Vault like copy, move, and search.
*   [vFlow (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/VerizonDigital/vflow) - High-performance, scalable and reliable IPFIX, sFlow and Netflow collector.
*   [wellington (‚≠ê302)](https://github.com/wellington/wellington) - Sass project management tool, extends the language with sprite functions (like Compass).
*   [woke (‚≠ê490)](https://github.com/get-woke/woke) - Detect non-inclusive language in your source code.

### Benchmarks / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [autobench (‚≠ê99)](https://github.com/davecheney/autobench) - Framework to compare the performance between different Go versions.
*   [go-benchmark-app (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app) - Powerful HTTP-benchmark tool mixed with –êb, Wrk, Siege tools. Gathering statistics and various parameters for benchmarks and comparison results.
*   [go-benchmarks (‚≠ê148)](https://github.com/tylertreat/go-benchmarks) - Few miscellaneous Go microbenchmarks. Compare some language features to alternative approaches.

*   [go-ml-benchmarks (‚≠ê32)](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/go-ml-benchmarks) - benchmarks for machine learning inference in Go.
*   [go-web-framework-benchmark (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark) - Go web framework benchmark.
*   [go\_serialization\_benchmarks (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/alecthomas/go_serialization_benchmarks) - Benchmarks of Go serialization methods.
*   [gocostmodel (‚≠ê61)](https://github.com/PuerkitoBio/gocostmodel) - Benchmarks of common basic operations for the Go language.
*   [golang-sql-benchmark](https://github.com/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark) - Collection of benchmarks for popular Go database/SQL utilities.
*   [gospeed (‚≠ê126)](https://github.com/feyeleanor/GoSpeed) - Go micro-benchmarks for calculating the speed of language constructs.
*   [kvbench (‚≠ê26)](https://github.com/jimrobinson/kvbench) - Key/Value database benchmark.
*   [skynet (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/atemerev/skynet) - Skynet 1M threads microbenchmark.
*   [speedtest-resize (‚≠ê243)](https://github.com/fawick/speedtest-resize) - Compare various Image resize algorithms for the Go language.
